===== src/hooks/useAppState.ts =====
     1	import { useReducer, useCallback, useEffect } from 'react';
     2	import type { AppState, AppAction, ImageSlice } from '../types';
     3	import {
     4	  loadState,
     5	  saveState,
     6	  createDebouncedSave,
     7	  type PersistableState,
     8	} from '../utils/persistence';
     9	
    10	// 创建防抖保存函数
    11	const debouncedSave = createDebouncedSave(500);
    12	
    13	// 从持久化存储加载初始状态
    14	function createInitialState(): AppState {
    15	  const persistedState = loadState();
    16	
    17	  return {
    18	    worker: null,
    19	    blobs: [],
    20	    objectUrls: [],
    21	    originalImage: null,
    22	    imageSlices: [],
    23	    selectedSlices: new Set<number>(),
    24	    isProcessing: false,
    25	    splitHeight: persistedState?.splitHeight ?? 1200,
    26	    fileName: persistedState?.fileName ?? '分割结果',
    27	  };
    28	}
    29	
    30	const initialState: AppState = createInitialState();
    31	
    32	// 状态reducer
    33	function appStateReducer(state: AppState, action: AppAction): AppState {
    34	  switch (action.type) {
    35	    case 'SET_WORKER':
    36	      return { ...state, worker: action.payload };
    37	
    38	    case 'ADD_BLOB': {
    39	      const newBlobs = [...state.blobs];
    40	      newBlobs[action.payload.index] = action.payload.blob;
    41	      return { ...state, blobs: newBlobs };
    42	    }
    43	
    44	    case 'SET_ORIGINAL_IMAGE':
    45	      return { ...state, originalImage: action.payload };
    46	
    47	    case 'ADD_IMAGE_SLICE': {
    48	      console.log('[AppState] 添加图片切片 action 被调用:', action.payload);
    49	      // 按 index 写入（而非按异步到达顺序 push），修复 img.onload 回调导致的切片乱序（spec §5）
    50	      const newImageSlices = [...state.imageSlices];
    51	      newImageSlices[action.payload.index] = action.payload;
    52	      const newState = {
    53	        ...state,
    54	        imageSlices: newImageSlices,
    55	        objectUrls: [...state.objectUrls, action.payload.url],
    56	      };
    57	      console.log('[AppState] 新状态中的 imageSlices 数量:', newState.imageSlices.length);
    58	      console.log('[AppState] 新状态中的 imageSlices:', newState.imageSlices);
    59	      return newState;
    60	    }
    61	
    62	    case 'TOGGLE_SLICE_SELECTION': {
    63	      const newSelectedSlices = new Set(state.selectedSlices);
    64	      if (newSelectedSlices.has(action.payload)) {
    65	        newSelectedSlices.delete(action.payload);
    66	      } else {
    67	        newSelectedSlices.add(action.payload);
    68	      }
    69	      return { ...state, selectedSlices: newSelectedSlices };
    70	    }
    71	
    72	    case 'SELECT_ALL_SLICES': {
    73	      const allIndices = state.imageSlices.map(slice => slice.index);
    74	      return { ...state, selectedSlices: new Set(allIndices) };
    75	    }
    76	
    77	    case 'DESELECT_ALL_SLICES':
    78	      return { ...state, selectedSlices: new Set<number>() };
    79	
    80	    case 'SET_PROCESSING':
    81	      return { ...state, isProcessing: action.payload };
    82	
    83	    case 'SET_SPLIT_HEIGHT':
    84	      return { ...state, splitHeight: action.payload };
    85	
    86	    case 'SET_FILE_NAME':
    87	      return { ...state, fileName: action.payload };
    88	
    89	    case 'CLEANUP_SESSION':
    90	      // 清理所有Object URLs
    91	      state.objectUrls.forEach(url => {
    92	        try {
    93	          URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    94	        } catch (error) {
    95	          console.warn('[AppState] 释放 Object URL 失败:', error);
    96	        }
    97	      });
    98	
    99	      // 终止Worker
   100	      if (state.worker) {
   101	        try {
   102	          state.worker.terminate();
   103	        } catch (error) {
   104	          console.warn('[AppState] 终止 Worker 失败:', error);
   105	        }
   106	      }
   107	
   108	      return {
   109	        ...initialState,
   110	        splitHeight: state.splitHeight, // 保留用户设置
   111	        fileName: state.fileName, // 保留用户设置
   112	      };
   113	
   114	    case 'PROCESSING_COMPLETE':
   115	      return { ...state, isProcessing: false };
   116	
   117	    default:
   118	      return state;
   119	  }
   120	}
   121	
   122	export function useAppState() {
   123	  const [state, dispatch] = useReducer(appStateReducer, initialState);
   124	
   125	  // 自动保存可持久化的状态
   126	  useEffect(() => {
   127	    const persistableState: PersistableState = {
   128	      splitHeight: state.splitHeight,
   129	      fileName: state.fileName,
   130	    };
   131	
   132	    debouncedSave(persistableState);
   133	  }, [state.splitHeight, state.fileName]);
   134	
   135	  // 提供语言设置保存的辅助函数
   136	  const saveLanguagePreference = useCallback(
   137	    (language: string) => {
   138	      const currentState = loadState() || {
   139	        splitHeight: state.splitHeight,
   140	        fileName: state.fileName,
   141	      };
   142	      const updatedState: PersistableState = {
   143	        ...currentState,
   144	        language,
   145	      };
   146	      saveState(updatedState);
   147	    },
   148	    [state.splitHeight, state.fileName]
   149	  );
   150	
   151	  // Action creators
   152	  const setWorker = useCallback((worker: Worker | null) => {
   153	    dispatch({ type: 'SET_WORKER', payload: worker });
   154	  }, []);
   155	
   156	  const addBlob = useCallback((blob: Blob, index: number) => {
   157	    dispatch({ type: 'ADD_BLOB', payload: { blob, index } });
   158	  }, []);
   159	
   160	  const setOriginalImage = useCallback((image: HTMLImageElement | null) => {
   161	    dispatch({ type: 'SET_ORIGINAL_IMAGE', payload: image });
   162	  }, []);
   163	
   164	  const addImageSlice = useCallback((slice: ImageSlice) => {
   165	    dispatch({ type: 'ADD_IMAGE_SLICE', payload: slice });
   166	  }, []);
   167	
   168	  const toggleSliceSelection = useCallback((index: number) => {
   169	    dispatch({ type: 'TOGGLE_SLICE_SELECTION', payload: index });
   170	  }, []);
   171	
   172	  const selectAllSlices = useCallback(() => {
   173	    dispatch({ type: 'SELECT_ALL_SLICES' });
   174	  }, []);
   175	
   176	  const deselectAllSlices = useCallback(() => {
   177	    dispatch({ type: 'DESELECT_ALL_SLICES' });
   178	  }, []);
   179	
   180	  const setProcessing = useCallback((isProcessing: boolean) => {
   181	    dispatch({ type: 'SET_PROCESSING', payload: isProcessing });
   182	  }, []);
   183	
   184	  const setSplitHeight = useCallback((height: number) => {
   185	    dispatch({ type: 'SET_SPLIT_HEIGHT', payload: height });
   186	  }, []);
   187	
   188	  const setFileName = useCallback((name: string) => {
   189	    dispatch({ type: 'SET_FILE_NAME', payload: name });
   190	  }, []);
   191	
   192	  const cleanupSession = useCallback(() => {
   193	    dispatch({ type: 'CLEANUP_SESSION' });
   194	  }, []);
   195	
   196	  const processingComplete = useCallback(() => {
   197	    dispatch({ type: 'PROCESSING_COMPLETE' });
   198	  }, []);
   199	
   200	  // 调试用的状态快照
   201	  const getStateSnapshot = useCallback(() => {
   202	    return {
   203	      hasOriginalImage: !!state.originalImage,
   204	      blobsCount: state.blobs.length,
   205	      objectUrlsCount: state.objectUrls.length,
   206	      imageSlicesCount: state.imageSlices.length,
   207	      selectedSlicesCount: state.selectedSlices.size,
   208	      isProcessing: state.isProcessing,
   209	      hasWorker: !!state.worker,
   210	      splitHeight: state.splitHeight,
   211	      fileName: state.fileName,
   212	    };
   213	  }, [state]);
   214	
   215	  return {
   216	    state,
   217	    actions: {
   218	      setWorker,
   219	      addBlob,
   220	      setOriginalImage,
   221	      addImageSlice,
   222	      toggleSliceSelection,
   223	      selectAllSlices,
   224	      deselectAllSlices,
   225	      setProcessing,
   226	      setSplitHeight,
   227	      setFileName,
   228	      cleanupSession,
   229	      processingComplete,
   230	    },
   231	    utils: {
   232	      saveLanguagePreference,
   233	    },
   234	    getStateSnapshot,
   235	  };
   236	}

===== src/hooks/useImageProcessor.ts =====
     1	import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
     2	import type { ImageProcessorHookReturn, AppState } from '../types';
     3	import { useWorker } from './useWorker';
     4	
     5	interface UseImageProcessorProps {
     6	  state: AppState;
     7	  actions: {
     8	    addBlob: (blob: Blob, index: number) => void;
     9	    addImageSlice: (slice: any) => void;
    10	    cleanupSession: () => void;
    11	    setProcessing: (isProcessing: boolean) => void;
    12	    setFileName: (name: string) => void;
    13	    setWorker: (worker: Worker | null) => void;
    14	    setOriginalImage: (image: HTMLImageElement | null) => void;
    15	    processingComplete: () => void;
    16	  };
    17	}
    18	
    19	export function useImageProcessor({
    20	  state,
    21	  actions,
    22	}: UseImageProcessorProps): ImageProcessorHookReturn {
    23	  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);
    24	
    25	  // Worker回调函数
    26	  const handleProgress = useCallback((workerProgress: number) => {
    27	    setProgress(workerProgress);
    28	  }, []);
    29	
    30	  const handleChunk = useCallback(
    31	    (blob: Blob, index: number) => {
    32	      console.log('[ImageProcessor] 收到图片切片:', index, blob.size);
    33	      // 添加Blob到状态
    34	      actions.addBlob(blob, index);
    35	
    36	      // 创建Object URL并添加图片切片
    37	      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    38	      console.log('[ImageProcessor] 创建 Object URL:', url);
    39	
    40	      // 创建临时图片来获取尺寸
    41	      const img = new Image();
    42	      img.onload = () => {
    43	        console.log('[ImageProcessor] 图片加载完成，尺寸:', img.naturalWidth, img.naturalHeight);
    44	        console.log(
    45	          '[ImageProcessor] 添加图片切片到状态:',
    46	          index,
    47	          img.naturalWidth,
    48	          img.naturalHeight
    49	        );
    50	        const imageSlice = {
    51	          blob,
    52	          url,
    53	          index,
    54	          width: img.naturalWidth,
    55	          height: img.naturalHeight,
    56	        };
    57	        console.log('[ImageProcessor] 即将添加的图片切片对象:', imageSlice);
    58	        actions.addImageSlice(imageSlice);
    59	      };
    60	      img.onerror = error => {
    61	        console.error('[ImageProcessor] 图片加载失败:', error);
    62	      };
    63	      img.src = url;
    64	    },
    65	    [actions]
    66	  );
    67	
    68	  const handleDone = useCallback(() => {
    69	    console.log('[ImageProcessor] 图片处理完成');
    70	    actions.processingComplete();
    71	    setProgress(100);
    72	  }, [actions]);
    73	
    74	  const handleError = useCallback(
    75	    (message: string) => {
    76	      console.error('[ImageProcessor] Worker 错误:', message);
    77	      actions.setProcessing(false);
    78	      setProgress(0);
    79	    },
    80	    [actions]
    81	  );
    82	
    83	  // 使用Worker hook
    84	  const { createWorker, startProcessing } = useWorker({
    85	    onProgress: handleProgress,
    86	    onChunk: handleChunk,
    87	    onDone: handleDone,
    88	    onError: handleError,
    89	  });
    90	
    91	  // 处理图片
    92	  const processImage = useCallback(
    93	    async (file: File) => {
    94	      console.log('[ImageProcessor] 开始处理图片:', file.name);
    95	
    96	      // 清理之前的会话
    97	      actions.cleanupSession();
    98	      setProgress(0);
    99	
   100	      // 设置处理状态
   101	      actions.setProcessing(true);
   102	      actions.setFileName(file.name.replace(/\.[^/.]+$/, '') || '分割结果');
   103	
   104	      // 创建并设置原始图片
   105	      const img = new Image();
   106	      const imageUrl = URL.createObjectURL(file);
   107	
   108	      img.onload = () => {
   109	        console.log('[ImageProcessor] 原始图片加载完成，设置到状态中');
   110	        actions.setOriginalImage(img);
   111	        URL.revokeObjectURL(imageUrl); // 清理临时URL
   112	      };
   113	
   114	      img.onerror = error => {
   115	        console.error('[ImageProcessor] 原始图片加载失败:', error);
   116	        URL.revokeObjectURL(imageUrl);
   117	      };
   118	
   119	      img.src = imageUrl;
   120	
   121	      // 确保Worker已创建
   122	      createWorker();
   123	
   124	      // 等待一小段时间确保Worker创建完成
   125	      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 200));
   126	
   127	      // 开始处理
   128	      startProcessing(file, state.splitHeight);
   129	
   130	      console.log('[ImageProcessor] 已发送文件到 Worker，分割高度:', state.splitHeight);
   131	    },
   132	    [actions, createWorker, startProcessing, state.splitHeight]
   133	  );
   134	
   135	  return {
   136	    processImage,
   137	    progress,
   138	    isProcessing: state.isProcessing,
   139	  };
   140	}

===== src/hooks/useWorker.ts =====
     1	import { useCallback, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
     2	import type { WorkerMessage } from '../types';
     3	
     4	export interface UseWorkerOptions {
     5	  onProgress?: (progress: number) => void;
     6	  onChunk?: (blob: Blob, index: number) => void;
     7	  onDone?: () => void;
     8	  onError?: (message: string) => void;
     9	}
    10	
    11	export interface UseWorkerReturn {
    12	  worker: Worker | null;
    13	  isWorkerReady: boolean;
    14	  startProcessing: (file: File, splitHeight: number) => void;
    15	  terminateWorker: () => void;
    16	  createWorker: () => void;
    17	}
    18	
    19	/**
    20	 * Web Worker管理Hook
    21	 * 提供Worker的创建、通信、生命周期管理功能
    22	 */
    23	export function useWorker(options: UseWorkerOptions = {}): UseWorkerReturn {
    24	  const workerRef = useRef<Worker | null>(null);
    25	  const isWorkerReadyRef = useRef(false);
    26	
    27	  const { onProgress, onChunk, onDone, onError } = options;
    28	
    29	  // 创建Worker
    30	  const createWorker = useCallback(() => {
    31	    try {
    32	      // 终止现有Worker
    33	      if (workerRef.current) {
    34	        workerRef.current.terminate();
    35	        workerRef.current = null;
    36	        isWorkerReadyRef.current = false;
    37	      }
    38	
    39	      // 创建新Worker
    40	      // type: 'module' 必需：worker 通过 ESM import splitAnalyzer，classic worker 不支持顶层 import。
    41	      // Vite 据此在 dev 用 module worker、build 打包为 ES module chunk。
    42	      workerRef.current = new Worker(new URL('../workers/split.worker.js', import.meta.url), {
    43	        type: 'module',
    44	      });
    45	
    46	      // 设置消息监听器
    47	      workerRef.current.onmessage = (event: MessageEvent<WorkerMessage>) => {
    48	        const { type, progress, blob, index, message } = event.data;
    49	
    50	        switch (type) {
    51	          case 'progress':
    52	            if (progress !== undefined && onProgress) {
    53	              onProgress(progress);
    54	            }
    55	            break;
    56	
    57	          case 'chunk':
    58	            if (blob && index !== undefined && onChunk) {
    59	              onChunk(blob, index);
    60	            }
    61	            break;
    62	
    63	          case 'done':
    64	            if (onDone) {
    65	              onDone();
    66	            }
    67	            break;
    68	
    69	          case 'error':
    70	            if (message && onError) {
    71	              onError(message);
    72	            }
    73	            break;
    74	
    75	          default:
    76	            console.warn('[useWorker] 未知的消息类型:', type);
    77	        }
    78	      };
    79	
    80	      // 设置错误监听器
    81	      workerRef.current.onerror = error => {
    82	        console.error('[useWorker] Worker错误:', error);
    83	        if (onError) {
    84	          onError(`Worker错误: ${error.message}`);
    85	        }
    86	      };
    87	
    88	      // 设置消息错误监听器
    89	      workerRef.current.onmessageerror = error => {
    90	        console.error('[useWorker] Worker消息错误:', error);
    91	        if (onError) {
    92	          onError('Worker消息传递错误');
    93	        }
    94	      };
    95	
    96	      isWorkerReadyRef.current = true;
    97	      console.log('[useWorker] Worker创建成功');
    98	    } catch (error) {
    99	      console.error('[useWorker] 创建Worker失败:', error);
   100	      if (onError) {
   101	        onError(`创建Worker失败: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : '未知错误'}`);
   102	      }
   103	    }
   104	  }, [onProgress, onChunk, onDone, onError]);
   105	
   106	  // 终止Worker
   107	  const terminateWorker = useCallback(() => {
   108	    if (workerRef.current) {
   109	      try {
   110	        workerRef.current.terminate();
   111	        console.log('[useWorker] Worker已终止');
   112	      } catch (error) {
   113	        console.warn('[useWorker] 终止Worker时出错:', error);
   114	      } finally {
   115	        workerRef.current = null;
   116	        isWorkerReadyRef.current = false;
   117	      }
   118	    }
   119	  }, []);
   120	
   121	  // 开始处理
   122	  const startProcessing = useCallback(
   123	    (file: File, splitHeight: number) => {
   124	      if (!workerRef.current || !isWorkerReadyRef.current) {
   125	        console.error('[useWorker] Worker未就绪');
   126	        if (onError) {
   127	          onError('Worker未就绪，请先创建Worker');
   128	        }
   129	        return;
   130	      }
   131	
   132	      try {
   133	        workerRef.current.postMessage({ file, splitHeight });
   134	        console.log('[useWorker] 已发送处理请求到Worker');
   135	      } catch (error) {
   136	        console.error('[useWorker] 发送消息到Worker失败:', error);
   137	        if (onError) {
   138	          onError(`发送消息失败: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : '未知错误'}`);
   139	        }
   140	      }
   141	    },
   142	    [onError]
   143	  );
   144	
   145	  // 组件卸载时清理Worker
   146	  useEffect(() => {
   147	    return () => {
   148	      terminateWorker();
   149	    };
   150	  }, [terminateWorker]);
   151	
   152	  return {
   153	    worker: workerRef.current,
   154	    isWorkerReady: isWorkerReadyRef.current,
   155	    startProcessing,
   156	    terminateWorker,
   157	    createWorker,
   158	  };
   159	}

===== src/workers/split.worker.js =====
     1	// Message Contract (v1.1):
     2	// From Main to Worker: { file: File, splitHeight: number }
     3	// From Worker to Main:
     4	// - Progress: { type: 'progress', progress: number } // 0-100；分段：0-25 解码 / 25-30 内容感知分析 / 30-95 切片 / 100 完成
     5	// - Chunk:    { type: 'chunk', blob: Blob, index: number }
     6	// - Done:     { type: 'done' } // Simplified completion signal
     7	// - Error:    { type: 'error', message: string }
     8	//
     9	// 内容感知切割（spec §4）：解码后插入「分析」阶段，调用纯函数 splitAnalyzer
    10	// 得到切割点；有切割点则按点切，无则回退固定高度等分（绝不切得比现状差）。
    11	
    12	import { analyzeSplitPoints } from '../utils/splitAnalyzer';
    13	
    14	// Web Worker for handling image splitting operations
    15	// This worker runs in a separate thread to avoid blocking the UI
    16	
    17	/**
    18	 * 主消息监听器 - 接收来自主线程的消息
    19	 */
    20	self.onmessage = function (event) {
    21	  try {
    22	    const { file, splitHeight } = event.data;
    23	
    24	    // 参数验证
    25	    if (!file) {
    26	      self.postMessage({
    27	        type: 'error',
    28	        message: 'No file provided',
    29	      });
    30	      return;
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    if (!(file instanceof File)) {
    34	      self.postMessage({
    35	        type: 'error',
    36	        message: 'Invalid file object provided',
    37	      });
    38	      return;
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    if (!splitHeight || typeof splitHeight !== 'number' || splitHeight <= 0) {
    42	      self.postMessage({
    43	        type: 'error',
    44	        message: 'Invalid splitHeight provided. Must be a positive number.',
    45	      });
    46	      return;
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    // 验证文件类型
    50	    if (!file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
    51	      self.postMessage({
    52	        type: 'error',
    53	        message: 'File must be an image',
    54	      });
    55	      return;
    56	    }
    57	
    58	    console.log(`Worker received: ${file.name}, splitHeight: ${splitHeight}`);
    59	
    60	    // 开始图片处理流程
    61	    processImage(file, splitHeight);
    62	  } catch (error) {
    63	    console.error('Worker error:', error);
    64	    self.postMessage({
    65	      type: 'error',
    66	      message: `Worker processing error: ${error.message}`,
    67	    });
    68	  }
    69	};
    70	
    71	/**
    72	 * 图片处理主函数
    73	 * 流程：解码 → 全图绘制 → 内容感知分析（得切割点）→ 按切割点切片（无切割点则等分回退）
    74	 */
    75	async function processImage(file, splitHeight) {
    76	  try {
    77	    // 发送初始进度
    78	    self.postMessage({
    79	      type: 'progress',
    80	      progress: 0,
    81	    });
    82	
    83	    console.log('Starting image processing...');
    84	
    85	    // 使用 createImageBitmap 解码图片
    86	    console.log('Decoding image with createImageBitmap...');
    87	    const imageBitmap = await createImageBitmap(file);
    88	
    89	    console.log(
    90	      `Image decoded successfully. Dimensions: ${imageBitmap.width} x ${imageBitmap.height}`
    91	    );
    92	
    93	    // 创建 OffscreenCanvas 并设置其尺寸与原图一致
    94	    const canvas = new OffscreenCanvas(imageBitmap.width, imageBitmap.height);
    95	    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    96	
    97	    console.log(`OffscreenCanvas created with dimensions: ${canvas.width} x ${canvas.height}`);
    98	
    99	    // 将图片位图绘制到 OffscreenCanvas 上
   100	    ctx.drawImage(imageBitmap, 0, 0);
   101	
   102	    // 更新进度到 25% (图片解码和绘制完成)
   103	    self.postMessage({
   104	      type: 'progress',
   105	      progress: 25,
   106	    });
   107	
   108	    // 释放 imageBitmap 资源
   109	    imageBitmap.close();
   110	
   111	    // 内容感知分析：读取全图像素，计算切割点
   112	    // 注：当前为全图 getImageData（KISS）；大图（>4000px）分块读取为未来优化项（spec §4.6）
   113	    console.log('Analyzing content for split points...');
   114	    let splitPoints = [];
   115	    try {
   116	      const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
   117	      splitPoints = analyzeSplitPoints(imageData.data, canvas.width, canvas.height, {
   118	        targetHeight: splitHeight,
   119	      });
   120	      console.log(
   121	        `Content analysis done. splitPoints: ${JSON.stringify(splitPoints)} (mode: ${
   122	          splitPoints.length > 0 ? 'content-aware' : 'equal-split-fallback'
   123	        })`
   124	      );
   125	    } catch (analyzeError) {
   126	      // 分析任何异常 → 安全回退等分（绝不因分析失败而中断或劣化，spec §4.5）
   127	      console.warn('Content analysis failed, falling back to equal split:', analyzeError);
   128	      splitPoints = [];
   129	    }
   130	
   131	    // 更新进度到 30% (分析完成)
   132	    self.postMessage({
   133	      type: 'progress',
   134	      progress: 30,
   135	    });
   136	
   137	    // task-1.4: 按切割点切片（无切割点则等分回退）
   138	    console.log('Starting image splitting...');
   139	
   140	    const sliceBounds = computeSliceBounds(splitPoints, canvas.height, splitHeight);
   141	    const totalChunks = sliceBounds.length;
   142	    console.log(`Total chunks to create: ${totalChunks}`);
   143	
   144	    // 循环处理每个切片
   145	    for (let i = 0; i < totalChunks; i++) {
   146	      const [startY, endY] = sliceBounds[i];
   147	      const chunkHeight = endY - startY;
   148	
   149	      console.log(
   150	        `Processing chunk ${i + 1}/${totalChunks}, startY: ${startY}, height: ${chunkHeight}`
   151	      );
   152	
   153	      // 创建临时 OffscreenCanvas 用于当前切片
   154	      const chunkCanvas = new OffscreenCanvas(canvas.width, chunkHeight);
   155	      const chunkCtx = chunkCanvas.getContext('2d');
   156	
   157	      // 使用 drawImage 复制指定区域到临时 canvas
   158	      chunkCtx.drawImage(
   159	        canvas, // 源 canvas
   160	        0,
   161	        startY, // 源区域起始位置
   162	        canvas.width,
   163	        chunkHeight, // 源区域尺寸
   164	        0,
   165	        0, // 目标位置
   166	        canvas.width,
   167	        chunkHeight // 目标尺寸
   168	      );
   169	
   170	      // 转换为 Blob (JPEG 格式，质量 0.92——减轻截图文字边缘振铃伪影)
   171	      const blob = await convertToBlob(chunkCanvas, 'image/jpeg', 0.92);
   172	
   173	      console.log(`Chunk ${i + 1} blob created, size: ${blob.size} bytes`);
   174	
   175	      // 发送切片数据
   176	      self.postMessage({
   177	        type: 'chunk',
   178	        blob: blob,
   179	        index: i,
   180	      });
   181	
   182	      // 计算并发送进度 (30% 到 95%)
   183	      const progress = Math.round(30 + ((i + 1) / totalChunks) * 65);
   184	      self.postMessage({
   185	        type: 'progress',
   186	        progress: progress,
   187	      });
   188	
   189	      console.log(`Chunk ${i + 1}/${totalChunks} completed, progress: ${progress}%`);
   190	    }
   191	
   192	    console.log('Image splitting completed');
   193	
   194	    // task-1.5: 发送完成消息
   195	    console.log('Sending completion signal...');
   196	
   197	    // 更新进度到 100%
   198	    self.postMessage({
   199	      type: 'progress',
   200	      progress: 100,
   201	    });
   202	
   203	    // 发送简化的完成消息
   204	    self.postMessage({
   205	      type: 'done',
   206	    });
   207	
   208	    console.log('✅ All processing completed successfully');
   209	  } catch (error) {
   210	    console.error('Error in processImage:', error);
   211	    self.postMessage({
   212	      type: 'error',
   213	      message: `Image processing error: ${error.message}`,
   214	    });
   215	  }
   216	}
   217	
   218	/**
   219	 * 根据切割点计算切片边界 [[startY, endY], ...]（spec §4.5）
   220	 * - 有切割点：按切割点分段，保证每段落在内容空白带之间
   221	 * - 无切割点：回退固定高度等分（与原逻辑一致，绝不切得比现状差）
   222	 *
   223	 * @param {number[]} splitPoints 切割点 y 坐标数组（来自 splitAnalyzer）
   224	 * @param {number} imageHeight   图像总高度
   225	 * @param {number} splitHeight   等分回退时的固定页高
   226	 * @returns {Array<[number, number]>} 切片边界数组
   227	 */
   228	function computeSliceBounds(splitPoints, imageHeight, splitHeight) {
   229	  // 内容感知：按切割点分段
   230	  if (splitPoints.length > 0) {
   231	    const bounds = [];
   232	    let prev = 0;
   233	    for (const point of splitPoints) {
   234	      bounds.push([prev, point]);
   235	      prev = point;
   236	    }
   237	    bounds.push([prev, imageHeight]);
   238	    return bounds;
   239	  }
   240	
   241	  // 等分回退：固定高度等分（与原 split.worker.js 行为完全一致）
   242	  const bounds = [];
   243	  const totalChunks = Math.ceil(imageHeight / splitHeight);
   244	  for (let i = 0; i < totalChunks; i++) {
   245	    const startY = i * splitHeight;
   246	    const endY = Math.min(startY + splitHeight, imageHeight);
   247	    bounds.push([startY, endY]);
   248	  }
   249	  return bounds;
   250	}
   251	
   252	/**
   253	 * 将 OffscreenCanvas 转换为 Blob
   254	 * @param {OffscreenCanvas} canvas - 要转换的 canvas
   255	 * @param {string} type - 图片类型 (如 'image/jpeg')
   256	 * @param {number} quality - 图片质量 (0-1)，默认 0.92（减轻文字振铃伪影）
   257	 * @returns {Promise<Blob>} - 转换后的 Blob 对象
   258	 */
   259	async function convertToBlob(canvas, type = 'image/jpeg', quality = 0.92) {
   260	  return await canvas.convertToBlob({

===== src/utils/splitAnalyzer.ts =====
     1	/**
     2	 * 内容感知切割分析器（Content-Aware Split Analyzer）
     3	 *
     4	 * 设计依据：docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-25-content-aware-split-design.md §4
     5	 *
     6	 * 核心原则：算法与 I/O 分离。本模块全部为纯函数，无 DOM/canvas/Worker 依赖，
     7	 * 可独立单测。Worker 仅负责 decode/getImageData/drawImage 胶水并调用本模块。
     8	 *
     9	 * 流水线（spec §4.2 不变量）：
    10	 *   压成行信号 → 去噪 → 找空白带 → 页高驱动选点 → 最小间距保护 → 无解安全回退
    11	 *
    12	 * ⚠️ thresholdRatio / minBandHeight / smoothingWindow 为起始经验值（spec §4.4），
    13	 *    必须用真实长截图校准后回填，不可拍脑袋定死。
    14	 */
    15	
    16	/** 低变化水平带：一段连续的「内容空白」行区间 */
    17	export interface Band {
    18	  /** 起始行（inclusive） */
    19	  top: number;
    20	  /** 结束行（exclusive） */
    21	  bottom: number;
    22	  /** 带中心行，作为切割点候选 */
    23	  center: number;
    24	}
    25	
    26	/**
    27	 * 分析阶段全部可调参数（ratio 形式以适配不同尺寸图片）。
    28	 * 默认值见 DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS。
    29	 */
    30	export interface SplitOptions {
    31	  /** 目标页高（复用现有 splitHeight 语义） */
    32	  targetHeight: number;
    33	  /** 列降采样步长，越大越快、精度越低 */
    34	  columnStep: number;
    35	  /** 低变化阈值倍数：阈值 = mean(profile) × thresholdRatio */
    36	  thresholdRatio: number;
    37	  /** 平滑窗口大小（行），约一行行距；1 表示不平滑 */
    38	  smoothingWindow: number;
    39	  /** 空白带最小高度（行），用于过滤噪声细缝 */
    40	  minBandHeight: number;
    41	  /** 搜索范围占 targetHeight 的比例（±） */
    42	  searchWindowRatio: number;
    43	  /** 最小切割间距占 targetHeight 的比例，防碎页 */
    44	  mergeRatio: number;
    45	  /** 单页最小高度占 targetHeight 的比例，末页合并依据 */
    46	  minPageRatio: number;
    47	}
    48	
    49	/** 默认参数（spec §4.3，部分为起始经验值，待校准） */
    50	export const DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS: SplitOptions = {
    51	  targetHeight: 1200,
    52	  columnStep: 4,
    53	  thresholdRatio: 0.3,
    54	  smoothingWindow: 8,
    55	  minBandHeight: 8,
    56	  searchWindowRatio: 0.2,
    57	  mergeRatio: 0.5,
    58	  minPageRatio: 0.5,
    59	};
    60	
    61	/** chooseSplitPoints 的参数（已由 ratio 换算为像素绝对值） */
    62	export interface ChoosePointsOptions {
    63	  /** 目标页高 */
    64	  targetHeight: number;
    65	  /** 搜索范围（±像素） */
    66	  searchWindow: number;
    67	  /** 最小切割间距（像素） */
    68	  mergeThreshold: number;
    69	  /** 单页最小高度（像素） */
    70	  minPageHeight: number;
    71	  /** 图像总高度 */
    72	  imageHeight: number;
    73	}
    74	
    75	/**
    76	 * 计算行级水平变化率（spec §4.2 第 1 步）。
    77	 *
    78	 * 对每行 y：在采样列上累加水平相邻像素的【灰度差绝对值】。
    79	 * 灰度 = 0.299R + 0.587G + 0.114B；行变化率反映该行内容密度，
    80	 * 文字行高、空白行接近 0。变化率不依赖背景色检测，对多背景图更鲁棒。
    81	 *
    82	 * @param pixels   RGBA 像素数据（每像素 4 字节）
    83	 * @param width    图像宽度（像素）
    84	 * @param height   图像高度（像素）
    85	 * @param columnStep 列降采样步长（默认 4，计算量降至 1/columnStep）
    86	 * @returns 长度为 height 的数组，profile[y] = 第 y 行的总变化率
    87	 */
    88	export function computeVariationProfile(
    89	  pixels: Uint8ClampedArray | Uint8Array,
    90	  width: number,
    91	  height: number,
    92	  columnStep: number = DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS.columnStep
    93	): number[] {
    94	  const profile: number[] = new Array(height).fill(0);
    95	  const step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(columnStep));
    96	
    97	  for (let y = 0; y < height; y++) {
    98	    const rowBase = y * width;
    99	    let variation = 0;
   100	    // 采样列 x = step, 2·step, ...，比较像素 x 与其左邻 x-1 的灰度差
   101	    for (let x = step; x < width; x += step) {
   102	      const idxCurr = (rowBase + x) * 4;
   103	      const idxPrev = (rowBase + x - 1) * 4;
   104	      const grayCurr =
   105	        0.299 * pixels[idxCurr] + 0.587 * pixels[idxCurr + 1] + 0.114 * pixels[idxCurr + 2];
   106	      const grayPrev =
   107	        0.299 * pixels[idxPrev] + 0.587 * pixels[idxPrev + 1] + 0.114 * pixels[idxPrev + 2];
   108	      variation += Math.abs(grayCurr - grayPrev);
   109	    }
   110	    profile[y] = variation;
   111	  }
   112	  return profile;
   113	}
   114	
   115	/**
   116	 * 居中滑动平均平滑（spec §4.2 第 2 步）。
   117	 * 消除单行噪声；windowSize=1 时原样返回（不平滑）。边界处只取存在的邻居。
   118	 *
   119	 * @param profile    变化率曲线
   120	 * @param windowSize 窗口大小（行）；越大越平滑
   121	 */
   122	export function smooth(profile: number[], windowSize: number): number[] {
   123	  const len = profile.length;
   124	  if (len === 0) return [];
   125	
   126	  const window = Math.max(1, Math.floor(windowSize));
   127	  if (window === 1) return [...profile];
   128	
   129	  const half = Math.floor(window / 2);
   130	  const result: number[] = new Array(len);
   131	  for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) {
   132	    let sum = 0;
   133	    let count = 0;
   134	    for (let d = -half; d <= half; d++) {
   135	      const j = i + d;
   136	      if (j >= 0 && j < len) {
   137	        sum += profile[j];
   138	        count++;
   139	      }
   140	    }
   141	    result[i] = count > 0 ? sum / count : 0;
   142	  }
   143	  return result;
   144	}
   145	
   146	/**
   147	 * 找出连续的低变化水平带（spec §4.2 第 3 步）。
   148	 *
   149	 * 连续多行 variation < threshold 且宽度 ≥ minBandHeight 的区间记为一个 Band。
   150	 * center 取区间中点，作为切割点候选。
   151	 *
   152	 * @param profile      （平滑后的）变化率曲线
   153	 * @param threshold    低变化判定阈值（绝对值）
   154	 * @param minBandHeight 空白带最小高度，过滤噪声细缝
   155	 */
   156	export function findLowVariationBands(
   157	  profile: number[],
   158	  threshold: number,
   159	  minBandHeight: number
   160	): Band[] {
   161	  const bands: Band[] = [];
   162	  const len = profile.length;
   163	  const minHeight = Math.max(1, Math.floor(minBandHeight));
   164	
   165	  let y = 0;
   166	  while (y < len) {
   167	    if (profile[y] < threshold) {
   168	      const top = y;
   169	      while (y < len && profile[y] < threshold) {
   170	        y++;
   171	      }
   172	      const bottom = y; // exclusive
   173	      if (bottom - top >= minHeight) {
   174	        bands.push({ top, bottom, center: Math.floor((top + bottom) / 2) });
   175	      }
   176	    } else {
   177	      y++;
   178	    }
   179	  }
   180	  return bands;
   181	}
   182	
   183	/**
   184	 * 页高驱动选点（spec §4.2 第 4 步 + §4.5 边界）。
   185	 *
   186	 * 从 0 起每推进约 targetHeight，在 ±searchWindow 内选最近 band.center；
   187	 * 窗口内无合格 band → 该刀回退精确 targetHeight；相邻候选间距 < mergeThreshold
   188	 * → 丢弃（防碎页）；末页剩余 < minPageHeight → 删除末点（并入上页）。
   189	 *
   190	 * 安全原则：任何不确定情况回退等分，绝不切得比固定高度等分差。
   191	 *
   192	 * @returns 切割点 y 坐标数组（长度 = 切片数 - 1）；空数组表示不切
   193	 */
   194	export function chooseSplitPoints(bands: Band[], options: ChoosePointsOptions): number[] {
   195	  const { targetHeight, searchWindow, mergeThreshold, minPageHeight, imageHeight } = options;
   196	  const points: number[] = [];
   197	
   198	  // 图片不足以再切 → 整图作为唯一切片
   199	  if (imageHeight <= targetHeight) {
   200	    return [];
   201	  }
   202	
   203	  let cursor = 0;
   204	  while (cursor + targetHeight < imageHeight) {
   205	    const ideal = cursor + targetHeight;
   206	    const lo = ideal - searchWindow;
   207	    const hi = ideal + searchWindow;
   208	
   209	    // 在 [lo, hi] 内找离 ideal 最近的 band.center；无则回退精确 ideal
   210	    let candidate = ideal;
   211	    let bestDist = Infinity;
   212	    for (const band of bands) {
   213	      if (band.center >= lo && band.center <= hi) {
   214	        const dist = Math.abs(band.center - ideal);
   215	        if (dist < bestDist) {
   216	          bestDist = dist;
   217	          candidate = band.center;
   218	        }
   219	      }
   220	    }
   221	
   222	    // 防碎页：候选距上一刀过近则丢弃（cursor 仍按 ideal 推进，避免死循环）
   223	    if (points.length === 0 || candidate - points[points.length - 1] >= mergeThreshold) {
   224	      points.push(candidate);
   225	    }
   226	    cursor = ideal;
   227	  }
   228	
   229	  // 末页合并：剩余高度过小 → 删除末点并入上一页
   230	  if (points.length > 0 && imageHeight - points[points.length - 1] < minPageHeight) {
   231	    points.pop();
   232	  }
   233	
   234	  return points;
   235	}
   236	
   237	/**
   238	 * 内容感知切割分析入口（封装 spec §4.2 全流程）。
   239	 *
   240	 * Worker 调用此函数：传入全图像素 + 尺寸，返回切割点数组。
   241	 * 返回空数组表示「不切」（图片过短）或「无合格空白带需等分回退」——
   242	 * 调用方对空数组应回退到固定高度等分（spec §4.5）。
   243	 *
   244	 * @param pixels  RGBA 像素数据
   245	 * @param width   图像宽度
   246	 * @param height  图像高度
   247	 * @param options 可选参数覆盖（缺省用 DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS）
   248	 * @returns 切割点 y 坐标数组；空表示需等分回退或不切
   249	 */
   250	export function analyzeSplitPoints(
   251	  pixels: Uint8ClampedArray | Uint8Array,
   252	  width: number,
   253	  height: number,
   254	  options?: Partial<SplitOptions>
   255	): number[] {
   256	  const opts = { ...DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS, ...options };
   257	
   258	  // 图片短于目标页高 → 不切
   259	  if (height <= opts.targetHeight) {
   260	    return [];

===== src/utils/pdfExporter.ts =====
     1	import jsPDF from 'jspdf';
     2	import type { ImageSlice } from '../types';
     3	
     4	/**
     5	 * PDF导出配置选项
     6	 */
     7	export interface PDFExportOptions {
     8	  /** 页面方向 */
     9	  orientation?: 'portrait' | 'landscape';
    10	  /** 页面格式 */
    11	  format?: 'a4' | 'a3' | 'letter';
    12	  /** 图片质量 (0-1) */
    13	  quality?: number;
    14	  /** 页边距 (mm) */
    15	  margin?: number;
    16	  /** 是否自动调整图片大小 */
    17	  autoResize?: boolean;
    18	  /** 每页最大图片数量 */
    19	  imagesPerPage?: number;
    20	}
    21	
    22	/**
    23	 * 默认PDF导出配置
    24	 */
    25	const DEFAULT_OPTIONS: Required<PDFExportOptions> = {
    26	  orientation: 'portrait',
    27	  format: 'a4',
    28	  quality: 0.8,
    29	  margin: 10,
    30	  autoResize: true,
    31	  imagesPerPage: 1,
    32	};
    33	
    34	/**
    35	 * PDF导出器类
    36	 */
    37	export class PDFExporter {
    38	  private options: Required<PDFExportOptions>;
    39	
    40	  constructor(options: PDFExportOptions = {}) {
    41	    this.options = { ...DEFAULT_OPTIONS, ...options };
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  /**
    45	   * 导出图片切片为PDF
    46	   * @param imageSlices 图片切片数组
    47	   * @param selectedIndices 选中的切片索引
    48	   * @param fileName 文件名
    49	   * @param onProgress 进度回调
    50	   */
    51	  async exportToPDF(
    52	    imageSlices: ImageSlice[],
    53	    selectedIndices: Set<number>,
    54	    fileName: string = 'exported-images',
    55	    onProgress?: (progress: number) => void
    56	  ): Promise<void> {
    57	    try {
    58	      // 过滤选中的切片
    59	      const selectedSlices = imageSlices
    60	        .filter(slice => selectedIndices.has(slice.index))
    61	        .sort((a, b) => a.index - b.index);
    62	
    63	      if (selectedSlices.length === 0) {
    64	        throw new Error('没有选中的图片切片');
    65	      }
    66	
    67	      // 创建PDF文档
    68	      const pdf = new jsPDF({
    69	        orientation: this.options.orientation,
    70	        unit: 'mm',
    71	        format: this.options.format,
    72	      });
    73	
    74	      // 获取页面尺寸
    75	      const pageWidth = pdf.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
    76	      const pageHeight = pdf.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
    77	      const contentWidth = pageWidth - this.options.margin * 2;
    78	      const contentHeight = pageHeight - this.options.margin * 2;
    79	
    80	      let imagesOnCurrentPage = 0;
    81	
    82	      for (let i = 0; i < selectedSlices.length; i++) {
    83	        const slice = selectedSlices[i];
    84	
    85	        // 如果需要新页面
    86	        if (imagesOnCurrentPage >= this.options.imagesPerPage) {
    87	          pdf.addPage();
    88	          imagesOnCurrentPage = 0;
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        // 如果是第一张图片，不需要添加页面
    92	        if (i === 0) {
    93	          // 第一页已经存在
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        try {
    97	          // 将Blob转换为base64
    98	          const imageData = await this.blobToBase64(slice.blob);
    99	
   100	          // 计算图片尺寸
   101	          const { width, height } = this.calculateImageSize(
   102	            slice.width,
   103	            slice.height,
   104	            contentWidth,
   105	            contentHeight
   106	          );
   107	
   108	          // 计算图片位置（居中）
   109	          const x = this.options.margin + (contentWidth - width) / 2;
   110	          const y =
   111	            this.options.margin +
   112	            imagesOnCurrentPage * (contentHeight / this.options.imagesPerPage);
   113	
   114	          // 添加图片到PDF
   115	          pdf.addImage(imageData, 'JPEG', x, y, width, height, undefined, 'FAST');
   116	
   117	          imagesOnCurrentPage++;
   118	
   119	          // 更新进度
   120	          if (onProgress) {
   121	            const progress = Math.round(((i + 1) / selectedSlices.length) * 100);
   122	            onProgress(progress);
   123	          }
   124	        } catch (error) {
   125	          console.warn(`处理图片切片 ${slice.index} 时出错:`, error);
   126	          continue;
   127	        }
   128	      }
   129	
   130	      // 保存PDF
   131	      const pdfFileName = fileName.endsWith('.pdf') ? fileName : `${fileName}.pdf`;
   132	      pdf.save(pdfFileName);
   133	
   134	      console.log(`PDF导出完成: ${pdfFileName}`);
   135	    } catch (error) {
   136	      console.error('PDF导出失败:', error);
   137	      throw error;
   138	    }
   139	  }
   140	
   141	  /**
   142	   * 将Blob转换为base64字符串
   143	   */
   144	  private async blobToBase64(blob: Blob): Promise<string> {
   145	    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   146	      const reader = new FileReader();
   147	      reader.onload = () => {
   148	        const result = reader.result as string;
   149	        resolve(result);
   150	      };
   151	      reader.onerror = reject;
   152	      reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
   153	    });
   154	  }
   155	
   156	  /**
   157	   * 计算图片在PDF中的尺寸
   158	   */
   159	  private calculateImageSize(
   160	    originalWidth: number,
   161	    originalHeight: number,
   162	    maxWidth: number,
   163	    maxHeight: number
   164	  ): { width: number; height: number } {
   165	    if (!this.options.autoResize) {
   166	      return { width: originalWidth, height: originalHeight };
   167	    }
   168	
   169	    const aspectRatio = originalWidth / originalHeight;
   170	
   171	    let width = maxWidth;
   172	    let height = width / aspectRatio;
   173	
   174	    // 如果高度超出限制，按高度缩放
   175	    if (height > maxHeight) {
   176	      height = maxHeight;
   177	      width = height * aspectRatio;
   178	    }
   179	
   180	    return { width, height };
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  /**
   184	   * 更新导出选项
   185	   */
   186	  updateOptions(options: Partial<PDFExportOptions>): void {
   187	    this.options = { ...this.options, ...options };
   188	  }
   189	
   190	  /**
   191	   * 获取当前配置
   192	   */
   193	  getOptions(): Required<PDFExportOptions> {
   194	    return { ...this.options };
   195	  }
   196	}
   197	
   198	/**
   199	 * 创建默认PDF导出器实例
   200	 */
   201	export const createPDFExporter = (options?: PDFExportOptions) => {
   202	  return new PDFExporter(options);
   203	};
   204	
   205	/**
   206	 * 快速导出PDF（使用默认配置）
   207	 */
   208	export const exportToPDF = async (
   209	  imageSlices: ImageSlice[],
   210	  selectedIndices: Set<number>,
   211	  fileName?: string,
   212	  onProgress?: (progress: number) => void
   213	) => {
   214	  const exporter = createPDFExporter();
   215	  return exporter.exportToPDF(imageSlices, selectedIndices, fileName, onProgress);
   216	};

===== src/utils/zipExporter.ts =====
     1	import JSZip from 'jszip';
     2	import type { ImageSlice } from '../types';
     3	
     4	/**
     5	 * ZIP导出配置选项
     6	 */
     7	export interface ZIPExportOptions {
     8	  /** 压缩级别 (0-9) */
     9	  compressionLevel?: number;
    10	  /** 文件名格式 */
    11	  fileNameFormat?: 'index' | 'sequence' | 'custom';
    12	  /** 自定义文件名前缀 */
    13	  fileNamePrefix?: string;
    14	  /** 图片格式 */
    15	  imageFormat?: 'original' | 'jpeg' | 'png';
    16	  /** JPEG质量 (0-1) */
    17	  jpegQuality?: number;
    18	}
    19	
    20	/**
    21	 * 默认ZIP导出配置
    22	 */
    23	const DEFAULT_OPTIONS: Required<ZIPExportOptions> = {
    24	  compressionLevel: 6,
    25	  fileNameFormat: 'sequence',
    26	  fileNamePrefix: 'slice',
    27	  imageFormat: 'original',
    28	  jpegQuality: 0.8,
    29	};
    30	
    31	/**
    32	 * ZIP导出器类
    33	 */
    34	export class ZIPExporter {
    35	  private options: Required<ZIPExportOptions>;
    36	
    37	  constructor(options: ZIPExportOptions = {}) {
    38	    this.options = { ...DEFAULT_OPTIONS, ...options };
    39	  }
    40	
    41	  /**
    42	   * 导出图片切片为ZIP
    43	   */
    44	  async exportToZIP(
    45	    imageSlices: ImageSlice[],
    46	    selectedIndices: Set<number>,
    47	    fileName: string = 'exported-images',
    48	    onProgress?: (progress: number) => void
    49	  ): Promise<void> {
    50	    try {
    51	      const selectedSlices = imageSlices
    52	        .filter(slice => selectedIndices.has(slice.index))
    53	        .sort((a, b) => a.index - b.index);
    54	
    55	      if (selectedSlices.length === 0) {
    56	        throw new Error('没有选中的图片切片');
    57	      }
    58	
    59	      const zip = new JSZip();
    60	
    61	      for (let i = 0; i < selectedSlices.length; i++) {
    62	        const slice = selectedSlices[i];
    63	
    64	        try {
    65	          const imageFileName = this.generateFileName(slice, i);
    66	          const processedBlob = await this.processImageFormat(slice.blob);
    67	          zip.file(imageFileName, processedBlob);
    68	
    69	          if (onProgress) {
    70	            const progress = Math.round(((i + 1) / selectedSlices.length) * 80);
    71	            onProgress(progress);
    72	          }
    73	        } catch (error) {
    74	          console.warn(`处理图片切片 ${slice.index} 时出错:`, error);
    75	          continue;
    76	        }
    77	      }
    78	
    79	      if (onProgress) {
    80	        onProgress(85);
    81	      }
    82	
    83	      const zipBlob = await zip.generateAsync({
    84	        type: 'blob',
    85	        compression: 'DEFLATE',
    86	        compressionOptions: {
    87	          level: this.options.compressionLevel,
    88	        },
    89	      });
    90	
    91	      if (onProgress) {
    92	        onProgress(95);
    93	      }
    94	
    95	      const zipFileName = fileName.endsWith('.zip') ? fileName : `${fileName}.zip`;
    96	      this.downloadBlob(zipBlob, zipFileName);
    97	
    98	      if (onProgress) {
    99	        onProgress(100);
   100	      }
   101	
   102	      console.log(`ZIP导出完成: ${zipFileName}`);
   103	    } catch (error) {
   104	      console.error('ZIP导出失败:', error);
   105	      throw error;
   106	    }
   107	  }
   108	
   109	  private generateFileName(slice: ImageSlice, sequenceIndex: number): string {
   110	    const extension = this.getFileExtension(slice.blob.type);
   111	
   112	    switch (this.options.fileNameFormat) {
   113	      case 'index':
   114	        return `${this.options.fileNamePrefix}_${slice.index}.${extension}`;
   115	      case 'sequence':
   116	        return `${this.options.fileNamePrefix}_${String(sequenceIndex + 1).padStart(3, '0')}.${extension}`;
   117	      case 'custom':
   118	        return `${this.options.fileNamePrefix}_${slice.index}_${sequenceIndex + 1}.${extension}`;
   119	      default:
   120	        return `${this.options.fileNamePrefix}_${sequenceIndex + 1}.${extension}`;
   121	    }
   122	  }
   123	
   124	  private getFileExtension(mimeType: string): string {
   125	    switch (this.options.imageFormat) {
   126	      case 'jpeg':
   127	        return 'jpg';
   128	      case 'png':
   129	        return 'png';
   130	      case 'original':
   131	      default:
   132	        if (mimeType.includes('jpeg')) return 'jpg';
   133	        if (mimeType.includes('png')) return 'png';
   134	        if (mimeType.includes('gif')) return 'gif';
   135	        if (mimeType.includes('webp')) return 'webp';
   136	        return 'jpg';
   137	    }
   138	  }
   139	
   140	  private async processImageFormat(blob: Blob): Promise<Blob> {
   141	    if (this.options.imageFormat === 'original') {
   142	      return blob;
   143	    }
   144	
   145	    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   146	      const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
   147	      const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
   148	      const img = new Image();
   149	
   150	      img.onload = () => {
   151	        canvas.width = img.naturalWidth;
   152	        canvas.height = img.naturalHeight;
   153	
   154	        if (ctx) {
   155	          ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);
   156	
   157	          const outputFormat = this.options.imageFormat === 'jpeg' ? 'image/jpeg' : 'image/png';
   158	          const quality =
   159	            this.options.imageFormat === 'jpeg' ? this.options.jpegQuality : undefined;
   160	
   161	          canvas.toBlob(
   162	            convertedBlob => {
   163	              if (convertedBlob) {
   164	                resolve(convertedBlob);
   165	              } else {
   166	                reject(new Error('图片格式转换失败'));
   167	              }
   168	            },
   169	            outputFormat,
   170	            quality
   171	          );
   172	        } else {
   173	          reject(new Error('无法获取Canvas上下文'));
   174	        }
   175	
   176	        URL.revokeObjectURL(img.src);
   177	      };
   178	
   179	      img.onerror = () => {
   180	        URL.revokeObjectURL(img.src);
   181	        reject(new Error('图片加载失败'));
   182	      };
   183	
   184	      img.src = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
   185	    });
   186	  }
   187	
   188	  private downloadBlob(blob: Blob, fileName: string): void {
   189	    const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
   190	    const link = document.createElement('a');
   191	    link.href = url;
   192	    link.download = fileName;
   193	    link.style.display = 'none';
   194	
   195	    document.body.appendChild(link);
   196	    link.click();
   197	    document.body.removeChild(link);
   198	
   199	    setTimeout(() => {
   200	      URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
   201	    }, 1000);
   202	  }
   203	
   204	  updateOptions(options: Partial<ZIPExportOptions>): void {
   205	    this.options = { ...this.options, ...options };
   206	  }
   207	
   208	  getOptions(): Required<ZIPExportOptions> {
   209	    return { ...this.options };
   210	  }
   211	}
   212	
   213	export const createZIPExporter = (options?: ZIPExportOptions) => {
   214	  return new ZIPExporter(options);
   215	};
   216	
   217	export const exportToZIP = async (
   218	  imageSlices: ImageSlice[],
   219	  selectedIndices: Set<number>,
   220	  fileName?: string,
   221	  onProgress?: (progress: number) => void
   222	) => {
   223	  const exporter = createZIPExporter();
   224	  return exporter.exportToZIP(imageSlices, selectedIndices, fileName, onProgress);
   225	};

===== src/components/ExportControls.tsx =====
     1	/**
     2	 * 导出控制组件
     3	 * 提供PDF和ZIP导出功能
     4	 */
     5	
     6	import React, { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
     7	import { useI18nContext } from '../hooks/useI18nContext';
     8	import { useViewport } from '../hooks/useViewport';
     9	
    10	interface ImageSlice {
    11	  blob: Blob;
    12	  url: string;
    13	  index: number;
    14	  width: number;
    15	  height: number;
    16	}
    17	
    18	interface ExportControlsProps {
    19	  selectedSlices: number[];
    20	  slices: ImageSlice[];
    21	  onExport: (format: 'pdf' | 'zip', options?: any) => void;
    22	  disabled?: boolean;
    23	  className?: string;
    24	  enableTouchOptimization?: boolean;
    25	  showAdvancedOptions?: boolean;
    26	}
    27	
    28	interface ExportOptions {
    29	  format: 'pdf' | 'zip';
    30	  quality: number;
    31	  filename: string;
    32	  pdfOptions?: {
    33	    orientation: 'portrait' | 'landscape';
    34	    pageSize: 'A4' | 'A3' | 'Letter';
    35	    margin: number;
    36	  };
    37	  zipOptions?: {
    38	    compression: 'none' | 'low' | 'medium' | 'high';
    39	    imageFormat: 'png' | 'jpeg';
    40	  };
    41	}
    42	
    43	export const ExportControls: React.FC<ExportControlsProps> = ({
    44	  selectedSlices,
    45	  slices,
    46	  onExport,
    47	  disabled = false,
    48	  className = '',
    49	  enableTouchOptimization = true,
    50	  showAdvancedOptions = true,
    51	}) => {
    52	  const { t } = useI18nContext();
    53	  const viewport = useViewport();
    54	
    55	  const [exportFormat, setExportFormat] = useState<'pdf' | 'zip'>('pdf');
    56	  const [isExporting, setIsExporting] = useState(false);
    57	  const [showOptions, setShowOptions] = useState(!viewport.isMobile);
    58	
    59	  // 触摸反馈
    60	  const triggerHapticFeedback = useCallback(() => {
    61	    if (enableTouchOptimization && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
    62	      navigator.vibrate(10);
    63	    }
    64	  }, [enableTouchOptimization]);
    65	
    66	  const [exportOptions, setExportOptions] = useState<ExportOptions>({
    67	    format: 'pdf',
    68	    quality: 0.9,
    69	    filename: 'screenshot-slices',
    70	    pdfOptions: {
    71	      orientation: 'portrait',
    72	      pageSize: 'A4',
    73	      margin: 20,
    74	    },
    75	    zipOptions: {
    76	      compression: 'medium',
    77	      imageFormat: 'png',
    78	    },
    79	  });
    80	
    81	  // 处理导出
    82	  const handleExport = useCallback(async () => {
    83	    if (disabled || selectedSlices.length === 0) return;
    84	
    85	    triggerHapticFeedback();
    86	    setIsExporting(true);
    87	    try {
    88	      await onExport(exportFormat, {
    89	        ...exportOptions,
    90	        selectedSlices,
    91	        slices: selectedSlices.map(index => slices[index]),
    92	      });
    93	    } catch (error) {
    94	      console.error('Export failed:', error);
    95	    } finally {
    96	      setIsExporting(false);
    97	    }
    98	  }, [
    99	    disabled,
   100	    selectedSlices,
   101	    exportFormat,
   102	    exportOptions,
   103	    onExport,
   104	    slices,
   105	    triggerHapticFeedback,
   106	  ]);
   107	
   108	  // 切换格式
   109	  const handleFormatChange = useCallback(
   110	    (format: 'pdf' | 'zip') => {
   111	      setExportFormat(format);
   112	      updateExportOptions({ format });
   113	      triggerHapticFeedback();
   114	    },
   115	    [triggerHapticFeedback]
   116	  );
   117	
   118	  // 切换选项显示
   119	  const toggleOptions = useCallback(() => {
   120	    setShowOptions(!showOptions);
   121	    triggerHapticFeedback();
   122	  }, [showOptions, triggerHapticFeedback]);
   123	
   124	  // 更新导出选项
   125	  const updateExportOptions = useCallback((updates: Partial<ExportOptions>) => {
   126	    setExportOptions(prev => ({ ...prev, ...updates }));
   127	  }, []);
   128	
   129	  const canExport = selectedSlices.length > 0 && !disabled && !isExporting;
   130	  const mobileOptimizedClass = viewport.isMobile ? 'mobile-export-controls' : '';
   131	
   132	  return (
   133	    <div className={`export-controls ${className} ${mobileOptimizedClass}`}>
   134	      <div className={`export-header ${viewport.isMobile ? 'mb-6' : 'mb-4'}`}>
   135	        <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
   136	          <div>
   137	            <h3
   138	              className={`${viewport.isMobile ? 'text-xl' : 'text-lg'} font-semibold text-gray-800 mb-2`}
   139	            >
   140	              {t('export.title')}
   141	            </h3>
   142	            <p className={`${viewport.isMobile ? 'text-base' : 'text-sm'} text-gray-600`}>
   143	              {t('export.selectedSlicesInfo', { count: selectedSlices.length })}
   144	            </p>
   145	          </div>
   146	
   147	          {/* 移动端选项切换按钮 */}
   148	          {viewport.isMobile && showAdvancedOptions && (
   149	            <button
   150	              onClick={toggleOptions}
   151	              className="flex items-center px-3 py-2 text-sm text-blue-600 bg-blue-50 rounded-lg font-medium"
   152	              style={{
   153	                touchAction: 'manipulation',
   154	                WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
   155	              }}
   156	            >
   157	              <span>{showOptions ? '收起设置' : '展开设置'}</span>
   158	              <span
   159	                className={`ml-1 transform transition-transform ${showOptions ? 'rotate-180' : ''}`}
   160	              >
   161	                ▼
   162	              </span>
   163	            </button>
   164	          )}
   165	        </div>
   166	      </div>
   167	
   168	      {/* 快速导出按钮（移动端优先） */}
   169	      {viewport.isMobile && (
   170	        <div className="quick-export mb-6">
   171	          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
   172	            <button
   173	              onClick={() => {
   174	                handleFormatChange('pdf');
   175	                if (!showOptions) handleExport();
   176	              }}
   177	              disabled={!canExport}
   178	              className={`${
   179	                exportFormat === 'pdf'
   180	                  ? 'bg-blue-500 text-white border-blue-500'
   181	                  : 'bg-white text-blue-500 border-blue-500'
   182	              } border-2 rounded-xl p-4 font-medium text-center min-h-[60px] flex flex-col items-center justify-center transition-colors`}
   183	              style={{
   184	                touchAction: 'manipulation',
   185	                WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
   186	              }}
   187	            >
   188	              <span className="text-lg mb-1">📄</span>
   189	              <span className="text-sm">PDF</span>
   190	            </button>
   191	
   192	            <button
   193	              onClick={() => {
   194	                handleFormatChange('zip');
   195	                if (!showOptions) handleExport();
   196	              }}
   197	              disabled={!canExport}
   198	              className={`${
   199	                exportFormat === 'zip'
   200	                  ? 'bg-green-500 text-white border-green-500'
   201	                  : 'bg-white text-green-500 border-green-500'
   202	              } border-2 rounded-xl p-4 font-medium text-center min-h-[60px] flex flex-col items-center justify-center transition-colors`}
   203	              style={{
   204	                touchAction: 'manipulation',
   205	                WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
   206	              }}
   207	            >
   208	              <span className="text-lg mb-1">🗜️</span>
   209	              <span className="text-sm">ZIP</span>
   210	            </button>
   211	          </div>
   212	        </div>
   213	      )}
   214	
   215	      {/* 格式选择（桌面端或展开时显示） */}
   216	      {(!viewport.isMobile || showOptions) && (
   217	        <div className={`format-selection ${viewport.isMobile ? 'mb-6' : 'mb-4'}`}>
   218	          <label
   219	            className={`block ${viewport.isMobile ? 'text-base' : 'text-sm'} font-medium text-gray-700 mb-3`}
   220	          >
   221	            {t('export.formatLabel')}
   222	          </label>
   223	          <div
   224	            className={`format-options ${viewport.isMobile ? 'flex-col space-y-3' : 'flex gap-4'}`}
   225	          >
   226	            <label
   227	              className={`flex items-center ${viewport.isMobile ? 'p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg' : ''} cursor-pointer`}
   228	            >
   229	              <input
   230	                type="radio"
   231	                value="pdf"
   232	                checked={exportFormat === 'pdf'}
   233	                onChange={() => handleFormatChange('pdf')}
   234	                className={`${viewport.isMobile ? 'mr-3 w-5 h-5' : 'mr-2'}`}
   235	                disabled={disabled}
   236	                style={{
   237	                  touchAction: 'manipulation',
   238	                }}
   239	              />
   240	              <span className="flex items-center flex-1">
   241	                <span className={`${viewport.isMobile ? 'text-base font-medium' : ''}`}>
   242	                  {t('export.pdfOption')}
   243	                </span>
   244	                <span
   245	                  className={`ml-2 ${viewport.isMobile ? 'text-sm' : 'text-xs'} text-gray-500 ${viewport.isMobile ? 'block' : ''}`}
   246	                >
   247	                  {t('export.pdfDescription')}
   248	                </span>
   249	              </span>
   250	            </label>
   251	
   252	            <label
   253	              className={`flex items-center ${viewport.isMobile ? 'p-3 bg-gray-50 rounded-lg' : ''} cursor-pointer`}
   254	            >
   255	              <input
   256	                type="radio"
   257	                value="zip"
   258	                checked={exportFormat === 'zip'}
   259	                onChange={() => handleFormatChange('zip')}
   260	                className={`${viewport.isMobile ? 'mr-3 w-5 h-5' : 'mr-2'}`}

===== src/components/FileUploader.tsx =====
     1	/**
     2	/**
     3	 * 文件上传组件 - 移动端优化版
     4	 * 支持拖拽上传、点击选择文件和触摸友好界面
     5	 */
     6	
     7	import React, { useCallback, useState, useRef } from 'react';
     8	import { useI18nContext } from '../hooks/useI18nContext';
     9	import { useViewport } from '../hooks/useViewport';
    10	
    11	interface FileUploaderProps {
    12	  onFileSelect: (file: File) => void;
    13	  disabled?: boolean;
    14	  maxFileSize?: number;
    15	  supportedFormats?: string[];
    16	  className?: string;
    17	  isProcessing?: boolean;
    18	  progress?: number;
    19	  enableTouchOptimization?: boolean;
    20	}
    21	
    22	export const FileUploader: React.FC<FileUploaderProps> = ({
    23	  onFileSelect,
    24	  disabled = false,
    25	  maxFileSize = 30 * 1024 * 1024, // 30MB
    26	  supportedFormats = ['image/png', 'image/jpeg', 'image/jpg', 'image/webp'],
    27	  className = '',
    28	  isProcessing = false,
    29	  progress = 0,
    30	  enableTouchOptimization = true,
    31	}) => {
    32	  const { t } = useI18nContext();
    33	  const viewport = useViewport();
    34	  const [isDragOver, setIsDragOver] = useState(false);
    35	  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
    36	  const [isActive, setIsActive] = useState(false);
    37	  const fileInputRef = useRef<HTMLInputElement>(null);
    38	
    39	  // 触摸反馈
    40	  const triggerHapticFeedback = useCallback(
    41	    (type: 'light' | 'medium' | 'heavy' = 'light') => {
    42	      if (enableTouchOptimization && viewport.isMobile && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
    43	        const patterns = { light: 10, medium: 20, heavy: 30 };
    44	        navigator.vibrate(patterns[type]);
    45	      }
    46	    },
    47	    [enableTouchOptimization, viewport.isMobile]
    48	  );
    49	
    50	  // 验证文件
    51	  const validateFile = useCallback(
    52	    (file: File): string | null => {
    53	      if (file.size > maxFileSize) {
    54	        return t('upload.fileSizeError', { size: Math.round(maxFileSize / 1024 / 1024) });
    55	      }
    56	
    57	      if (!supportedFormats.includes(file.type)) {
    58	        const formats = supportedFormats.map(f => f.split('/')[1]).join(', ');
    59	        return t('upload.fileTypeError', { formats });
    60	      }
    61	
    62	      return null;
    63	    },
    64	    [maxFileSize, supportedFormats, t]
    65	  );
    66	
    67	  // 处理文件选择
    68	  const handleFileSelect = useCallback(
    69	    (file: File) => {
    70	      setError(null);
    71	
    72	      const validationError = validateFile(file);
    73	      if (validationError) {
    74	        setError(validationError);
    75	        triggerHapticFeedback('heavy');
    76	        return;
    77	      }
    78	
    79	      triggerHapticFeedback('medium');
    80	      onFileSelect(file);
    81	    },
    82	    [validateFile, onFileSelect, triggerHapticFeedback]
    83	  );
    84	
    85	  // 处理拖拽事件
    86	  const handleDragOver = useCallback(
    87	    (e: React.DragEvent) => {
    88	      e.preventDefault();
    89	      if (!disabled && !isProcessing) {
    90	        setIsDragOver(true);
    91	      }
    92	    },
    93	    [disabled, isProcessing]
    94	  );
    95	
    96	  const handleDragLeave = useCallback((e: React.DragEvent) => {
    97	    e.preventDefault();
    98	    setIsDragOver(false);
    99	  }, []);
   100	
   101	  const handleDrop = useCallback(
   102	    (e: React.DragEvent) => {
   103	      e.preventDefault();
   104	      setIsDragOver(false);
   105	
   106	      if (disabled || isProcessing) return;
   107	
   108	      const files = Array.from(e.dataTransfer.files);
   109	      if (files.length > 0) {
   110	        handleFileSelect(files[0]);
   111	      }
   112	    },
   113	    [disabled, isProcessing, handleFileSelect]
   114	  );
   115	
   116	  // 处理点击上传
   117	  const handleClick = useCallback(() => {
   118	    if (!disabled && !isProcessing && fileInputRef.current) {
   119	      triggerHapticFeedback('light');
   120	      fileInputRef.current.click();
   121	    }
   122	  }, [disabled, isProcessing, triggerHapticFeedback]);
   123	
   124	  // 处理触摸事件（移动端）
   125	  const handleTouchStart = useCallback(() => {
   126	    if (!disabled && !isProcessing) {
   127	      setIsActive(true);
   128	      triggerHapticFeedback('light');
   129	    }
   130	  }, [disabled, isProcessing, triggerHapticFeedback]);
   131	
   132	  const handleTouchEnd = useCallback(() => {
   133	    setIsActive(false);
   134	  }, []);
   135	
   136	  const handleInputChange = useCallback(
   137	    (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement>) => {
   138	      const files = e.target.files;
   139	      if (files && files.length > 0) {
   140	        handleFileSelect(files[0]);
   141	      }
   142	    },
   143	    [handleFileSelect]
   144	  );
   145	
   146	  // 移动端样式
   147	  const mobileOptimizedClass = viewport.isMobile ? 'mobile-file-uploader' : '';
   148	  const isDisabled = disabled || isProcessing;
   149	
   150	  return (
   151	    <div className={`file-uploader ${className} ${mobileOptimizedClass}`}>
   152	      {/* 上传区域 */}
   153	      <div
   154	        className={`
   155	          upload-area border-2 border-dashed rounded-lg text-center cursor-pointer transition-all duration-200
   156	          ${viewport.isMobile ? 'p-8 min-h-[200px]' : 'p-6 min-h-[160px]'}
   157	          ${
   158	            isDragOver
   159	              ? 'border-blue-500 bg-blue-50 scale-[1.02]'
   160	              : isActive
   161	                ? 'border-blue-400 bg-blue-25 scale-[0.98]'
   162	                : 'border-gray-300 hover:border-gray-400 hover:bg-gray-50'
   163	          }
   164	          ${isDisabled ? 'opacity-50 cursor-not-allowed' : ''}
   165	          ${viewport.isMobile ? 'active:scale-[0.98] shadow-sm' : ''}
   166	        `}
   167	        onDragOver={handleDragOver}
   168	        onDragLeave={handleDragLeave}
   169	        onDrop={handleDrop}
   170	        onClick={handleClick}
   171	        onTouchStart={handleTouchStart}
   172	        onTouchEnd={handleTouchEnd}
   173	        style={{
   174	          touchAction: 'manipulation',
   175	          WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
   176	          userSelect: 'none',
   177	          WebkitUserSelect: 'none',
   178	        }}
   179	      >
   180	        {/* 上传图标 */}
   181	        <div className={`upload-icon ${viewport.isMobile ? 'text-5xl mb-4' : 'text-4xl mb-4'}`}>
   182	          {isProcessing ? '⏳' : isDragOver ? '📥' : '📤'}
   183	        </div>
   184	
   185	        {/* 上传文字 */}
   186	        <div className="upload-text">
   187	          {isProcessing ? (
   188	            <div className="processing-state">
   189	              <p
   190	                className={`${viewport.isMobile ? 'text-xl' : 'text-lg'} font-medium text-blue-600 mb-3`}
   191	              >
   192	                {t('upload.processing')}
   193	              </p>
   194	              {progress > 0 && (
   195	                <div className="progress-container mb-4">
   196	                  <div className="w-full bg-gray-200 rounded-full h-2">
   197	                    <div
   198	                      className="bg-blue-500 h-2 rounded-full transition-all duration-300"
   199	                      style={{ width: `${progress}%` }}
   200	                    ></div>
   201	                  </div>
   202	                  <p className="text-sm text-gray-600 mt-2">{Math.round(progress)}%</p>
   203	                </div>
   204	              )}
   205	            </div>
   206	          ) : (
   207	            <div className="upload-state">
   208	              <p
   209	                className={`${viewport.isMobile ? 'text-xl' : 'text-lg'} font-medium text-gray-700 mb-3`}
   210	              >
   211	                {isDragOver
   212	                  ? t('upload.dropToUpload')
   213	                  : viewport.isMobile
   214	                    ? t('upload.tapToUpload')
   215	                    : t('upload.dragText')}
   216	              </p>
   217	
   218	              {/* 移动端额外提示 */}
   219	              {viewport.isMobile && !isDragOver && (
   220	                <div className="mobile-instructions mb-4">
   221	                  <div className="flex items-center justify-center space-x-4 text-gray-500">
   222	                    <span className="flex items-center text-sm">
   223	                      <span className="mr-1">👆</span>
   224	                      {t('upload.tapInstruction')}
   225	                    </span>
   226	                    {/* 如果支持文件API，显示相机选项 */}
   227	                    {'capture' in HTMLInputElement.prototype && (
   228	                      <span className="flex items-center text-sm">
   229	                        <span className="mr-1">📷</span>
   230	                        {t('upload.cameraOption')}
   231	                      </span>
   232	                    )}
   233	                  </div>
   234	                </div>
   235	              )}
   236	
   237	              <p className={`${viewport.isMobile ? 'text-base' : 'text-sm'} text-gray-500`}>
   238	                {t('upload.supportedFormats', {
   239	                  formats: supportedFormats.map(f => f.split('/')[1].toUpperCase()).join(', '),
   240	                  maxSize: Math.round(maxFileSize / 1024 / 1024),
   241	                })}
   242	              </p>
   243	            </div>
   244	          )}
   245	        </div>
   246	
   247	        {/* 隐藏的文件输入 */}
   248	        <input
   249	          ref={fileInputRef}
   250	          type="file"
   251	          accept={supportedFormats.join(',')}
   252	          onChange={handleInputChange}
   253	          className="hidden"
   254	          disabled={isDisabled}
   255	          /* 移动端支持相机拍照 */
   256	          capture={viewport.isMobile ? 'environment' : undefined}
   257	        />
   258	      </div>
   259	
   260	      {/* 移动端快捷按钮 */}

===== src/components/ScreenshotSplitter.tsx =====
     1	/**
     2	 * 截图分割器主组件 - 移动端优化版
     3	 * 整合文件上传、图片处理、预览和导出功能
     4	 * 响应式设计，支持触摸友好界面
     5	 */
     6	
     7	import React, { useState, useCallback, useMemo } from 'react';
     8	import { FileUploader } from './FileUploader';
     9	import { ImagePreview } from './ImagePreview';
    10	import { ExportControls } from './ExportControls';
    11	import { useImageProcessor } from '../hooks/useImageProcessor';
    12	import { useAppState } from '../hooks/useAppState';
    13	import { useDebugState } from '../hooks/useDebugState';
    14	import { useViewport } from '../hooks/useViewport';
    15	import { DebugPanel } from './DebugPanel';
    16	
    17	interface ScreenshotSplitterProps {
    18	  className?: string;
    19	  onStateChange?: (state: any) => void;
    20	  maxFileSize?: number;
    21	  supportedFormats?: string[];
    22	  enableTouchOptimization?: boolean;
    23	}
    24	
    25	export const ScreenshotSplitter: React.FC<ScreenshotSplitterProps> = ({
    26	  className = '',
    27	  onStateChange,
    28	  maxFileSize = 10 * 1024 * 1024, // 10MB
    29	  supportedFormats = ['image/png', 'image/jpeg', 'image/jpg', 'image/webp'],
    30	  enableTouchOptimization = true,
    31	}) => {
    32	  const [currentFile, setCurrentFile] = useState<File | null>(null);
    33	  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
    34	
    35	  const { state, actions } = useAppState();
    36	  const { processImage, isProcessing } = useImageProcessor({ state, actions });
    37	  const viewport = useViewport();
    38	
    39	  // 触摸反馈
    40	  const triggerHapticFeedback = useCallback(
    41	    (type: 'light' | 'medium' | 'heavy' = 'light') => {
    42	      if (enableTouchOptimization && viewport.isMobile && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
    43	        const patterns = { light: 10, medium: 20, heavy: 30 };
    44	        navigator.vibrate(patterns[type]);
    45	      }
    46	    },
    47	    [enableTouchOptimization, viewport.isMobile]
    48	  );
    49	
    50	  // 添加调试状态Hook
    51	  const debugState = useDebugState({
    52	    state,
    53	    originalImage: state.originalImage,
    54	    slices: state.imageSlices,
    55	    selectedSlices: Array.from(state.selectedSlices),
    56	    isProcessing: isProcessing || state.isProcessing,
    57	  });
    58	
    59	  // 处理文件上传
    60	  const handleFileUpload = useCallback(
    61	    async (file: File) => {
    62	      try {
    63	        setError(null);
    64	        setCurrentFile(file);
    65	        triggerHapticFeedback('medium');
    66	
    67	        // 验证文件大小
    68	        if (file.size > maxFileSize) {
    69	          throw new Error(`文件大小不能超过 ${Math.round(maxFileSize / 1024 / 1024)}MB`);
    70	        }
    71	
    72	        // 验证文件格式
    73	        if (!supportedFormats.includes(file.type)) {
    74	          throw new Error(`不支持的文件格式，请上传 ${supportedFormats.join(', ')} 格式的图片`);
    75	        }
    76	
    77	        // 处理图片
    78	        await processImage(file);
    79	
    80	        // 通知父组件状态变化
    81	        onStateChange?.(state);
    82	      } catch (err) {
    83	        const errorMessage = err instanceof Error ? err.message : '文件处理失败';
    84	        setError(errorMessage);
    85	        triggerHapticFeedback('heavy');
    86	        console.error('File upload error:', err);
    87	      }
    88	    },
    89	    [maxFileSize, supportedFormats, processImage, onStateChange, state, triggerHapticFeedback]
    90	  );
    91	
    92	  // 处理切片选择
    93	  const handleSliceSelection = useCallback(
    94	    (selectedIndices: number[]) => {
    95	      // 清除当前选择
    96	      actions.deselectAllSlices();
    97	      // 添加新选择
    98	      selectedIndices.forEach(index => {
    99	        actions.toggleSliceSelection(index);
   100	      });
   101	      triggerHapticFeedback('light');
   102	      onStateChange?.(state);
   103	    },
   104	    [actions, onStateChange, state, triggerHapticFeedback]
   105	  );
   106	
   107	  // 处理导出
   108	  const handleExport = useCallback(
   109	    (format: 'pdf' | 'zip', options?: any) => {
   110	      // 导出逻辑将在ExportControls组件中处理
   111	      triggerHapticFeedback('medium');
   112	      console.log('Export requested:', format, options);
   113	    },
   114	    [triggerHapticFeedback]
   115	  );
   116	
   117	  // 重置状态
   118	  const handleReset = useCallback(() => {
   119	    setCurrentFile(null);
   120	    setError(null);
   121	    actions.cleanupSession();
   122	    triggerHapticFeedback('light');
   123	    onStateChange?.(state);
   124	  }, [actions, onStateChange, state, triggerHapticFeedback]);
   125	
   126	  // 计算组件状态
   127	  const componentState = useMemo(
   128	    () => ({
   129	      hasFile: Boolean(currentFile),
   130	      hasSlices: state.imageSlices.length > 0,
   131	      hasSelection: state.selectedSlices.size > 0,
   132	      isProcessing: isProcessing || state.isProcessing,
   133	      canExport: state.selectedSlices.size > 0 && !isProcessing,
   134	    }),
   135	    [
   136	      currentFile,
   137	      state.imageSlices.length,
   138	      state.selectedSlices.size,
   139	      isProcessing,
   140	      state.isProcessing,
   141	    ]
   142	  );
   143	
   144	  // 移动端样式类
   145	  const mobileOptimizedClass = viewport.isMobile ? 'mobile-screenshot-splitter' : '';
   146	
   147	  return (
   148	    <div className={`screenshot-splitter ${className} ${mobileOptimizedClass}`}>
   149	      {/* 错误提示 - 移动端优化 */}
   150	      {error && (
   151	        <div
   152	          className={`error-message bg-red-100 border border-red-400 text-red-700 rounded ${
   153	            viewport.isMobile ? 'px-4 py-4 mb-6 text-base' : 'px-4 py-3 mb-4 text-sm'
   154	          }`}
   155	        >
   156	          <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
   157	            <div className="flex items-start flex-1">
   158	              <span className="text-lg mr-2 flex-shrink-0">⚠️</span>
   159	              <div>
   160	                <strong className={viewport.isMobile ? 'text-base' : 'text-sm'}>错误：</strong>
   161	                <span className="ml-1">{error}</span>
   162	                {/* 移动端错误处理提示 */}
   163	                {viewport.isMobile && (
   164	                  <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-red-600">
   165	                    💡 请检查文件格式和大小，或尝试选择其他图片
   166	                  </p>
   167	                )}
   168	              </div>
   169	            </div>
   170	            <button
   171	              onClick={() => setError(null)}
   172	              className={`text-red-700 hover:text-red-900 font-bold ${
   173	                viewport.isMobile ? 'text-xl p-1 min-w-[44px] min-h-[44px]' : 'text-lg'
   174	              }`}
   175	              style={{
   176	                touchAction: 'manipulation',
   177	                WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
   178	              }}
   179	            >
   180	              ×
   181	            </button>
   182	          </div>
   183	        </div>
   184	      )}
   185	
   186	      {/* 文件上传区域 - 移动端优化 */}
   187	      <div className={`upload-section ${viewport.isMobile ? 'mb-8' : 'mb-6'}`}>
   188	        <FileUploader
   189	          onFileSelect={handleFileUpload}
   190	          disabled={componentState.isProcessing}
   191	          maxFileSize={maxFileSize}
   192	          supportedFormats={supportedFormats}
   193	          enableTouchOptimization={enableTouchOptimization}
   194	          isProcessing={componentState.isProcessing}
   195	        />
   196	      </div>
   197	
   198	      {/* 处理状态指示器 - 移动端优化 */}
   199	      {componentState.isProcessing && (
   200	        <div
   201	          className={`processing-indicator bg-blue-100 border border-blue-400 text-blue-700 rounded ${
   202	            viewport.isMobile ? 'px-5 py-4 mb-8' : 'px-4 py-3 mb-4'
   203	          }`}
   204	        >
   205	          <div className="flex items-center justify-center">
   206	            <div
   207	              className={`animate-spin rounded-full border-b-2 border-blue-700 mr-3 ${
   208	                viewport.isMobile ? 'h-6 w-6' : 'h-4 w-4'
   209	              }`}
   210	            ></div>
   211	            <span className={viewport.isMobile ? 'text-base font-medium' : 'text-sm'}>
   212	              正在处理图片，请稍候...
   213	            </span>
   214	          </div>
   215	          {/* 移动端处理提示 */}
   216	          {viewport.isMobile && (
   217	            <p className="text-sm text-blue-600 mt-2 text-center">
   218	              📱 图片较大时处理时间可能较长，请耐心等待
   219	            </p>
   220	          )}
   221	        </div>
   222	      )}
   223	
   224	      {/* 图片预览区域 - 移动端优化 */}
   225	      {(componentState.hasSlices || state.imageSlices.length > 0) && (
   226	        <div className={`preview-section ${viewport.isMobile ? 'mb-8' : 'mb-6'}`}>
   227	          <ImagePreview
   228	            originalImage={state.originalImage}
   229	            slices={state.imageSlices}
   230	            selectedSlices={Array.from(state.selectedSlices)}
   231	            onSelectionChange={handleSliceSelection}
   232	            enableTouchOptimization={enableTouchOptimization}
   233	          />
   234	        </div>
   235	      )}
   236

   240	          <ExportControls
   241	            selectedSlices={Array.from(state.selectedSlices)}
