   244	            disabled={!componentState.canExport}
   245	            enableTouchOptimization={enableTouchOptimization}
   246	          />
   247	        </div>

   251	      <div

   253	          viewport.isMobile ? 'flex-col space-y-4' : 'flex gap-4 items-center'
   254	        }`}
   255	      >
   256	        {componentState.hasFile && (
   257	          <button
   258	            onClick={handleReset}
   259	            className={`
   260	              reset-button bg-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-600 active:bg-gray-700 text-white rounded transition-colors

===== src/components/Navigation.tsx =====
     1	/**
     2	 * 导航组件 - 性能优化版本
     3	 * 使用React.memo、useCallback等优化技术减少不必要的重渲染
     4	 */
     5	
     6	import React, { memo, useCallback, useMemo, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
     7	import { useNavigationState } from '../hooks/useNavigationState';
     8	import { usePerformanceMonitor } from '../utils/navigationPerformanceMonitor';
     9	import { CompactLanguageSwitcher } from './LanguageSwitcher';
    10	import { useI18nContext } from '../hooks/useI18nContext';
    11	import { useViewport } from '../hooks/useViewport';
    12	import { useSwipeGestures } from '../hooks/useSwipeGestures';
    13	import { TouchNav } from './mobile/TouchNav';
    14	import './Navigation.css';
    15	
    16	// 导航项接口
    17	interface NavigationItem {
    18	  path: string;
    19	  name: string;
    20	  icon?: string;
    21	  disabled?: boolean;
    22	  active?: boolean;
    23	}
    24	
    25	// 导航组件Props接口
    26	interface NavigationProps {
    27	  appState: any;
    28	  currentPath: string;
    29	  onNavigate: (path: string) => void;
    30	  className?: string;
    31	  showProgress?: boolean;
    32	  showTooltips?: boolean;
    33	  mobileOptimized?: boolean;
    34	  enableSwipeNavigation?: boolean;
    35	  hapticFeedback?: boolean;
    36	}
    37	
    38	// 单个导航按钮组件 - 使用memo优化，添加触摸优化
    39	const NavigationButton = memo<{
    40	  item: NavigationItem;
    41	  onNavigate: (path: string) => void;
    42	  showTooltips?: boolean;
    43	  isMobile?: boolean;
    44	  hapticFeedback?: boolean;
    45	}>(({ item, onNavigate, showTooltips = true, isMobile = false, hapticFeedback = true }) => {
    46	  const { t } = useI18nContext();
    47	  // 性能监控
    48	  const performanceMonitor = usePerformanceMonitor('NavigationButton');
    49	
    50	  // 触摸反馈功能
    51	  const triggerHapticFeedback = useCallback(() => {
    52	    if (hapticFeedback && 'vibrate' in navigator) {
    53	      navigator.vibrate(10);
    54	    }
    55	  }, [hapticFeedback]);
    56	
    57	  // 优化点击处理函数，使用useCallback避免重新创建
    58	  const handleClick = useCallback(
    59	    (e: React.MouseEvent) => {
    60	      e.preventDefault();
    61	
    62	      if (item.disabled) {
    63	        return;
    64	      }
    65	
    66	      // 触摸反馈
    67	      triggerHapticFeedback();
    68	
    69	      // 记录交互性能
    70	      performanceMonitor.recordInteraction('button-click', 0);
    71	
    72	      onNavigate(item.path);
    73	    },
    74	    [item.disabled, item.path, onNavigate, performanceMonitor, triggerHapticFeedback]
    75	  );
    76	
    77	  // 优化键盘处理函数
    78	  const handleKeyDown = useCallback(
    79	    (e: React.KeyboardEvent) => {
    80	      if (e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' ') {
    81	        e.preventDefault();
    82	        handleClick(e as any);
    83	      }
    84	    },
    85	    [handleClick]
    86	  );
    87	
    88	  // 计算按钮类名，使用useMemo优化
    89	  const buttonClassName = useMemo(() => {
    90	    const classes = ['nav-button'];
    91	
    92	    if (item.active) classes.push('active');
    93	    if (item.disabled) classes.push('disabled');
    94	    if (isMobile) classes.push('mobile-optimized');
    95	
    96	    return classes.join(' ');
    97	  }, [item.active, item.disabled, isMobile]);
    98	
    99	  // 计算按钮样式 - 移动端优化
   100	  const buttonStyle = useMemo(() => {
   101	    if (!isMobile) return undefined;
   102	
   103	    return {
   104	      minWidth: '44px',
   105	      minHeight: '44px',
   106	      padding: '12px 16px',
   107	      fontSize: '14px',
   108	      fontWeight: '500',
   109	      borderRadius: '12px',
   110	      touchAction: 'manipulation',
   111	      WebkitTapHighlightColor: 'transparent',
   112	      transition: 'all 0.2s cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
   113	    } as React.CSSProperties;
   114	  }, [isMobile]);
   115	
   116	  // 计算按钮状态文本，用于无障碍访问
   117	  const ariaLabel = useMemo(() => {
   118	    let label = item.name;
   119	    if (item.active) label += ` (${t('navigation.accessibility.current')})`;
   120	    if (item.disabled) label += ` (${t('navigation.accessibility.disabled')})`;
   121	    return label;
   122	  }, [item.name, item.active, item.disabled, t]);
   123	
   124	  return (
   125	    <button
   126	      className={buttonClassName}
   127	      style={buttonStyle}
   128	      onClick={handleClick}
   129	      onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
   130	      disabled={item.disabled}
   131	      aria-label={ariaLabel}
   132	      title={showTooltips ? ariaLabel : undefined}
   133	      tabIndex={item.disabled ? -1 : 0}
   134	    >
   135	      {item.icon && (
   136	        <span className="nav-icon" aria-hidden="true">
   137	          {item.icon}
   138	        </span>
   139	      )}
   140	      <span className="nav-text">{item.name}</span>
   141	    </button>
   142	  );
   143	});
   144	
   145	NavigationButton.displayName = 'NavigationButton';
   146	
   147	// 进度条组件 - 使用memo优化
   148	const ProgressBar = memo<{
   149	  percentage: number;
   150	  totalSteps: number;
   151	  completedSteps: number;
   152	}>(({ percentage, totalSteps, completedSteps }) => {
   153	  const { t } = useI18nContext();
   154	  const progressStyle = useMemo(
   155	    () => ({
   156	      width: `${percentage}%`,
   157	    }),
   158	    [percentage]
   159	  );
   160	
   161	  return (
   162	    <div
   163	      className="nav-progress"
   164	      role="progressbar"
   165	      aria-valuenow={percentage}
   166	      aria-valuemin={0}
   167	      aria-valuemax={100}
   168	    >
   169	      <div className="nav-progress-bar" style={progressStyle} />
   170	      <span className="nav-progress-text" aria-live="polite">
   171	        {t('navigation.progress.completed', {
   172	          completed: completedSteps,
   173	          total: totalSteps,
   174	          percentage,
   175	        })}
   176	      </span>
   177	    </div>
   178	  );
   179	});
   180	
   181	ProgressBar.displayName = 'ProgressBar';
   182	
   183	// 主导航组件 - 使用memo优化，添加移动端支持
   184	const Navigation = memo<NavigationProps>(
   185	  ({
   186	    appState,
   187	    currentPath,
   188	    onNavigate,
   189	    className = '',
   190	    showProgress = true,
   191	    showTooltips = true,
   192	    mobileOptimized = true,
   193	    enableSwipeNavigation = true,
   194	    hapticFeedback = true,
   195	  }) => {
   196	    const { t } = useI18nContext();
   197	    const viewport = useViewport();
   198	    // 性能监控
   199	    const performanceMonitor = usePerformanceMonitor('Navigation');
   200	
   201	    // 移动端自适应状态
   202	    const [isMobileView, setIsMobileView] = useState(false);
   203	
   204	    useEffect(() => {
   205	      setIsMobileView(mobileOptimized && viewport.isMobile);
   206	    }, [mobileOptimized, viewport.isMobile]);
   207	
   208	    // 使用优化的导航状态Hook
   209	    const {
   210	      navigationItems,
   211	      navigationMetrics,
   212	      canGoNext,
   213	      canGoPrevious,
   214	      getNextAvailableStep,
   215	      getPreviousAvailableStep,
   216	    } = useNavigationState(appState, currentPath);
   217	
   218	    // 优化导航处理函数，使用useCallback
   219	    const handleNavigate = useCallback(
   220	      (path: string) => {
   221	        performanceMonitor.recordInteraction('navigation', 1);
   222	        onNavigate(path);
   223	      },
   224	      [onNavigate, performanceMonitor]
   225	    );
   226	
   227	    // 快捷导航函数
   228	    const handleNext = useCallback(() => {
   229	      const nextStep = getNextAvailableStep();
   230	      if (nextStep) {
   231	        handleNavigate(nextStep);
   232	      }
   233	    }, [getNextAvailableStep, handleNavigate]);
   234	
   235	    const handlePrevious = useCallback(() => {
   236	      const prevStep = getPreviousAvailableStep();
   237	      if (prevStep) {
   238	        handleNavigate(prevStep);
   239	      }
   240	    }, [getPreviousAvailableStep, handleNavigate]);
   241	
   242	    // 滑动手势处理（移动端）
   243	    const swipeHandlers = useSwipeGestures(
   244	      {
   245	        onSwipeLeft: useCallback(() => {
   246	          if (enableSwipeNavigation && canGoNext) {
   247	            handleNext();
   248	          }
   249	        }, [enableSwipeNavigation, canGoNext, handleNext]),
   250	
   251	        onSwipeRight: useCallback(() => {
   252	          if (enableSwipeNavigation && canGoPrevious) {
   253	            handlePrevious();
   254	          }
   255	        }, [enableSwipeNavigation, canGoPrevious, handlePrevious]),
   256	      },
   257	      {
   258	        minDistance: 50,
   259	        maxDuration: 500,
   260	        preventDefault: true,

===== src/hooks/useNavigationState.ts =====
     1	/**
     2	 * 导航状态Hook - 优化版本
     3	 * 使用React性能优化技术，减少不必要的重渲染
     4	 */
     5	
     6	import { useState, useEffect, useMemo, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';
     7	
     8	// 临时AppState接口定义，直到正确导入
     9	interface AppState {
    10	  originalImage: HTMLImageElement | null;
    11	  imageSlices: any[];
    12	  selectedSlices: Set<number>;
    13	  isProcessing?: boolean;
    14	  [key: string]: any;
    15	}
    16	
    17	// 导航状态接口
    18	export interface NavigationState {
    19	  currentStep: string;
    20	  availableSteps: string[];
    21	  completedSteps: string[];
    22	  blockedSteps: string[];
    23	}
    24	
    25	// 导航项接口
    26	export interface NavigationItem {
    27	  path: string;
    28	  name: string;
    29	  icon?: string;
    30	  disabled?: boolean;
    31	  active?: boolean;
    32	}
    33	
    34	// 导航指标接口
    35	export interface NavigationMetrics {
    36	  totalSteps: number;
    37	  completedSteps: number;
    38	  currentStepIndex: number;
    39	  progressPercentage: number;
    40	}
    41	
    42	// 默认导航项 - 使用键名，实际显示文本通过国际化处理
    43	const DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS: NavigationItem[] = [
    44	  { path: '/', name: 'navigation.home', icon: '🏠' },
    45	  { path: '/upload', name: 'navigation.upload', icon: '📤' },
    46	  { path: '/split', name: 'navigation.split', icon: '✂️' },
    47	  { path: '/export', name: 'navigation.export', icon: '💾' },
    48	];
    49	
    50	/**
    51	 * 优化的导航状态Hook
    52	 */
    53	export function useNavigationState(
    54	  appState: AppState,
    55	  currentPath: string = '/',
    56	  options: {
    57	    enableValidation?: boolean;
    58	    onStateChange?: (state: NavigationState) => void;
    59	  } = {}
    60	) {
    61	  const { enableValidation = true, onStateChange } = options;
    62	
    63	  const [navigationState, setNavigationState] = useState<NavigationState>({
    64	    currentStep: currentPath,
    65	    availableSteps: ['/'],
    66	    completedSteps: [],
    67	    blockedSteps: ['/split', '/export'],
    68	  });
    69	
    70	  // 使用ref来存储上一次的依赖值，避免不必要的计算
    71	  const prevDepsRef = useRef<
    72	    | {
    73	        hasOriginalImage: boolean;
    74	        imageSlicesLength: number;
    75	        selectedSlicesSize: number;
    76	        currentPath: string;
    77	        isProcessing: boolean;
    78	      }
    79	    | undefined
    80	  >(undefined);
    81	
    82	  // 计算关键状态，使用useMemo优化
    83	  const keyStates = useMemo(() => {
    84	    const hasOriginalImage = !!appState.originalImage;
    85	    const imageSlicesLength = appState.imageSlices.length;
    86	    const selectedSlicesSize = appState.selectedSlices.size;
    87	    const isProcessing = appState.isProcessing || false;
    88	
    89	    return {
    90	      hasOriginalImage,
    91	      hasImageSlices: imageSlicesLength > 0,
    92	      hasSelectedSlices: selectedSlicesSize > 0,
    93	      imageSlicesLength,
    94	      selectedSlicesSize,
    95	      isProcessing,
    96	    };
    97	  }, [
    98	    appState.originalImage,
    99	    appState.imageSlices.length,
   100	    appState.selectedSlices.size,
   101	    appState.isProcessing,
   102	  ]);
   103	
   104	  // 计算导航项状态，使用useMemo优化
   105	  const navigationItems = useMemo(() => {
   106	    const { hasOriginalImage, hasSelectedSlices, isProcessing } = keyStates;
   107	
   108	    return DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS.map(item => {
   109	      let disabled = false;
   110	      const active = currentPath === item.path;
   111	
   112	      // 根据路径和应用状态确定是否禁用
   113	      switch (item.path) {
   114	        case '/':
   115	        case '/upload':
   116	          disabled = isProcessing;
   117	          break;
   118	        case '/split':
   119	          disabled = !hasOriginalImage || isProcessing;
   120	          break;
   121	        case '/export':
   122	          disabled = !hasSelectedSlices || isProcessing;
   123	          break;
   124	        default:
   125	          disabled = isProcessing;
   126	      }
   127	
   128	      return {
   129	        ...item,
   130	        disabled,
   131	        active,
   132	      };
   133	    });
   134	  }, [keyStates, currentPath]);
   135	
   136	  // 计算导航状态，使用useMemo优化
   137	  const computedNavigationState = useMemo(() => {
   138	    const { hasOriginalImage, hasImageSlices, hasSelectedSlices } = keyStates;
   139	
   140	    const completedSteps: string[] = [];
   141	    const availableSteps: string[] = [];
   142	    const blockedSteps: string[] = [];
   143	
   144	    DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS.forEach(item => {
   145	      const navItem = navigationItems.find(ni => ni.path === item.path);
   146	
   147	      if (navItem?.disabled) {
   148	        blockedSteps.push(item.path);
   149	      } else if (navItem?.active) {
   150	        availableSteps.push(item.path);
   151	      } else {
   152	        // 判断是否为已完成步骤
   153	        switch (item.path) {
   154	          case '/':
   155	            completedSteps.push(item.path);
   156	            break;
   157	          case '/upload':
   158	            if (hasOriginalImage) {
   159	              completedSteps.push(item.path);
   160	            } else {
   161	              availableSteps.push(item.path);
   162	            }
   163	            break;
   164	          case '/split':
   165	            if (hasImageSlices) {
   166	              completedSteps.push(item.path);
   167	            } else if (hasOriginalImage) {
   168	              availableSteps.push(item.path);
   169	            }
   170	            break;
   171	          case '/export':
   172	            if (hasSelectedSlices) {
   173	              availableSteps.push(item.path);
   174	            }
   175	            break;
   176	        }
   177	      }
   178	    });
   179	
   180	    return {
   181	      currentStep: currentPath,
   182	      availableSteps,
   183	      completedSteps,
   184	      blockedSteps,
   185	    };
   186	  }, [keyStates, navigationItems, currentPath]);
   187	
   188	  // 只在关键依赖变化时更新状态
   189	  useEffect(() => {
   190	    const currentDeps = {
   191	      hasOriginalImage: keyStates.hasOriginalImage,
   192	      imageSlicesLength: keyStates.imageSlicesLength,
   193	      selectedSlicesSize: keyStates.selectedSlicesSize,
   194	      currentPath,
   195	      isProcessing: keyStates.isProcessing,
   196	    };
   197	
   198	    // 浅比较，避免不必要的更新
   199	    const prevDeps = prevDepsRef.current;
   200	    if (
   201	      !prevDeps ||
   202	      prevDeps.hasOriginalImage !== currentDeps.hasOriginalImage ||
   203	      prevDeps.imageSlicesLength !== currentDeps.imageSlicesLength ||
   204	      prevDeps.selectedSlicesSize !== currentDeps.selectedSlicesSize ||
   205	      prevDeps.currentPath !== currentDeps.currentPath ||
   206	      prevDeps.isProcessing !== currentDeps.isProcessing
   207	    ) {
   208	      setNavigationState(computedNavigationState);
   209	      prevDepsRef.current = currentDeps;
   210	
   211	      // 调用状态变化回调
   212	      if (onStateChange) {
   213	        onStateChange(computedNavigationState);
   214	      }
   215	    }
   216	  }, [computedNavigationState, keyStates, currentPath, onStateChange]);
   217	
   218	  // 计算导航指标，使用useMemo优化
   219	  const navigationMetrics = useMemo((): NavigationMetrics => {
   220	    const totalSteps = DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS.length;
   221	    const completedSteps = computedNavigationState.completedSteps.length;
   222	    const currentStepIndex = DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS.findIndex(item => item.path === currentPath);
   223	    const progressPercentage = Math.round((completedSteps / totalSteps) * 100);
   224	
   225	    return {
   226	      totalSteps,
   227	      completedSteps,
   228	      currentStepIndex: currentStepIndex >= 0 ? currentStepIndex : 0,
   229	      progressPercentage,
   230	    };
   231	  }, [computedNavigationState, currentPath]);
   232	
   233	  // 获取下一个可用步骤
   234	  const getNextAvailableStep = useCallback((): string | null => {
   235	    const currentIndex = DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS.findIndex(item => item.path === currentPath);
   236	
   237	    for (let i = currentIndex + 1; i < DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS.length; i++) {
   238	      const item = DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS[i];
   239	      const navItem = navigationItems.find(ni => ni.path === item.path);
   240	      if (navItem && !navItem.disabled) {
   241	        return item.path;
   242	      }
   243	    }
   244	
   245	    return null;
   246	  }, [currentPath, navigationItems]);
   247	
   248	  // 获取上一个可用步骤
   249	  const getPreviousAvailableStep = useCallback((): string | null => {
   250	    const currentIndex = DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS.findIndex(item => item.path === currentPath);
   251	
   252	    for (let i = currentIndex - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
   253	      const item = DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS[i];
   254	      const navItem = navigationItems.find(ni => ni.path === item.path);
   255	      if (navItem && !navItem.disabled) {
   256	        return item.path;
   257	      }
   258	    }
   259	
   260	    return null;

===== src/components/SEOManager.tsx =====
     1	import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useCallback, useRef, useState } from 'react';
     2	import { Helmet, HelmetProvider } from 'react-helmet-async';

    16	/**
    17	 * 性能优化钩子
    18	 * 监控页面性能并优化SEO元数据加载
    19	 */
    20	const useSEOPerformance = () => {
    21	  const [metrics, setMetrics] = useState<PerformanceMetrics | null>(null);
    22	  const observerRef = useRef<PerformanceObserver | null>(null);
    23	
    24	  useEffect(() => {
    25	    // 创建性能观察器
    26	    if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && 'PerformanceObserver' in window) {
    27	      try {
    28	        observerRef.current = new PerformanceObserver(list => {
    29	          const entries = list.getEntries();
    30	          let fcp = 0,
    31	            lcp = 0,
    32	            fid = 0,
    33	            cls = 0,
    34	            ttfb = 0;
    35	
    36	          entries.forEach(entry => {
    37	            if (entry.name === 'first-contentful-paint') {
    38	              fcp = entry.startTime;
    39	            } else if (entry.entryType === 'largest-contentful-paint') {
    40	              lcp = entry.startTime;
    41	            } else if (entry.entryType === 'first-input') {
    42	              fid = (entry as any).processingStart - entry.startTime;
    43	            } else if (entry.entryType === 'layout-shift') {
    44	              cls += (entry as any).value;
    45	            } else if (entry.entryType === 'navigation') {
    46	              ttfb = (entry as any).responseStart;
    47	            }
    48	          });
    49	
    50	          setMetrics({ fcp, lcp, fid, cls, ttfb });
    51	        });
    52	
    53	        // 观察多种性能指标
    54	        observerRef.current.observe({
    55	          entryTypes: [
    56	            'paint',
    57	            'largest-contentful-paint',
    58	            'first-input',
    59	            'layout-shift',
    60	            'navigation',
    61	          ],
    62	        });
    63	      } catch (error) {
    64	        console.warn('Performance observation not supported:', error);
    65	      }
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    return () => {
    69	      if (observerRef.current) {
    70	        observerRef.current.disconnect();
    71	      }
    72	    };
    73	  }, []);
    74	
    75	  return metrics;
    76	};
    77	
    78	/**
    79	 * 视窗检测钩子
    80	 * 检测设备类型和视窗信息以优化元数据
    81	 */
    82	const useViewportDetection = (): ViewportInfo => {
    83	  const [viewportInfo, setViewportInfo] = useState<ViewportInfo>({
    84	    width: 0,
    85	    height: 0,
    86	    deviceType: 'desktop',
    87	    isMobile: false,
    88	    isTablet: false,
    89	    isDesktop: true,
    90	    orientation: 'landscape',
    91	  });
    92	
    93	  useEffect(() => {
    94	    const updateViewport = () => {
    95	      const width = window.innerWidth;
    96	      const height = window.innerHeight;
    97	      const isMobile = width < 768;
    98	      const isTablet = width >= 768 && width < 1024;
    99	      const isDesktop = width >= 1024;
   100	
   101	      setViewportInfo({
   102	        width,
   103	        height,
   104	        deviceType: isMobile ? 'mobile' : isTablet ? 'tablet' : 'desktop',
   105	        isMobile,
   106	        isTablet,
   107	        isDesktop,
   108	        orientation: width > height ? 'landscape' : 'portrait',
   109	      });
   110	    };
   111	
   112	    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
   113	      updateViewport();
   114	      window.addEventListener('resize', updateViewport);
   115	      window.addEventListener('orientationchange', updateViewport);
   116	
   117	      return () => {
   118	        window.removeEventListener('resize', updateViewport);
   119	        window.removeEventListener('orientationchange', updateViewport);
   120	      };
   121	    }
   122	  }, []);
   123	
   124	  return viewportInfo;
   125	};
   126

   152	        }
   153	      } catch (error) {

   158

   168	      language,
   169	      context,
   170	      customMetadata,
   171	      viewport: viewportInfo.deviceType,
   172	    });
   173	
   174	    // 避免不必要的重新计算
   175	    if (previousContext.current === contextKey) return;
   176	    previousContext.current = contextKey;
   177

   190

   193	        const dynamicDescription = addContextToDescription(baseDescription, context, language);
   194	
   195	        // 设备优化
   196	        const deviceOptimized = optimizeForDevice(
   197	          { title: dynamicTitle, description: dynamicDescription },
   198	          viewportInfo.deviceType
   199	        );
   200	
   201	        metadata = {
   202	          title: deviceOptimized.title,
   203	          description: deviceOptimized.description,
   204	          keywords: pageConfig.keywords,
   205	          ogTitle: deviceOptimized.title,
   206	          ogDescription: deviceOptimized.description,
   207	          ogImage:
   208	            config.defaultImages?.ogImage ||
   209	            `${config.site?.url || SEO_CONFIG.siteUrl}/og-image.png`,
   210	          ogType: 'website' as const,
   211	          ogUrl: `${config.site?.url || SEO_CONFIG.siteUrl}${getPagePath(page, language)}`,
   212	          twitterCard: 'summary_large_image' as const,
   213	          twitterTitle: deviceOptimized.title,
   214	          twitterDescription: deviceOptimized.description,
   215	          twitterImage:

   220	          robots: 'index,follow',

   225	          modifiedTime: customMetadata.modifiedTime || new Date().toISOString(),

   227	        };
   228	      } else {

   231	
   232	        // 应用设备优化
   233	        const deviceOptimized = optimizeForDevice(

   235	          viewportInfo.deviceType
   236	        );
   237

   239	        metadata.description = deviceOptimized.description;

   243	        metadata.twitterDescription = deviceOptimized.description;
   244	      }
   245	
   246	      setDynamicMetadata(metadata);

   249	      // 回退到基础元数据
   250	      setDynamicMetadata(generatePageMetadata(page, context, language, customMetadata));
   251	    }
   252	  }, [config, page, language, context, customMetadata, viewportInfo.deviceType]);
   253	
   254	  return dynamicMetadata;
   255	};

===== src/components/EnhancedSEOManager.tsx =====
     1	import React, { useEffect, useMemo, useRef, useState, lazy, Suspense } from 'react';
     2	import { Helmet, HelmetProvider } from 'react-helmet-async';
     3	import { generatePageMetadata } from '../utils/seo/metadataGenerator';
     4	import '../config/seo.config';
     5	import '../utils/seo/SEOConfigManager';
     6	// import { useSEOConfig } from '../hooks/useSEOConfig';
     7	import { useViewport } from '../hooks/useViewport';
     8	import type {
     9	  SEOManagerProps,
    10	  SEOMetadata,
    11	  Language,
    12	  PageType,
    13	  ViewportInfo,
    14	  PerformanceMetrics,
    15	  StructuredDataType,
    16	} from '../types/seo.types';
    17	
    18	// Lazy load structured data generator for performance
    19	const StructuredDataProvider = lazy(() =>
    20	  import('./seo/StructuredDataProvider').then(module => ({
    21	    default: module.StructuredDataProvider,
    22	  }))
    23	);
    24	
    25	/**
    26	 * Enhanced Performance Hook with Core Web Vitals
    27	 */
    28	const useEnhancedSEOPerformance = (enabled: boolean = true) => {
    29	  const [metrics, setMetrics] = useState<PerformanceMetrics>({
    30	    fcp: 0,
    31	    lcp: 0,
    32	    fid: 0,
    33	    cls: 0,
    34	    ttfb: 0,
    35	  });
    36	  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
    37	  const observersRef = useRef<PerformanceObserver[]>([]);
    38	  const metricsBufferRef = useRef<Partial<PerformanceMetrics>>({});
    39	
    40	  useEffect(() => {
    41	    if (!enabled || typeof window === 'undefined' || !('PerformanceObserver' in window)) {
    42	      setIsLoading(false);
    43	      return;
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    let isMounted = true;
    47	
    48	    // Import web-vitals dynamically for better performance
    49	    import('web-vitals')
    50	      .then(({ onCLS, onFCP, onINP, onLCP, onTTFB }) => {
    51	        if (!isMounted) return;
    52	
    53	        // Track Core Web Vitals with buffering
    54	        const updateMetric = (name: keyof PerformanceMetrics, value: number) => {
    55	          metricsBufferRef.current[name] = value;
    56	
    57	          // Batch updates using requestIdleCallback for better performance
    58	          if ('requestIdleCallback' in window) {
    59	            requestIdleCallback(() => {
    60	              if (isMounted) {
    61	                setMetrics(prev => ({
    62	                  ...prev,
    63	                  ...metricsBufferRef.current,
    64	                }));
    65	                metricsBufferRef.current = {};
    66	              }
    67	            });
    68	          } else {
    69	            setMetrics(prev => ({ ...prev, [name]: value }));
    70	          }
    71	        };
    72	
    73	        onCLS((metric: any) => updateMetric('cls', metric.value));
    74	        onFCP((metric: any) => updateMetric('fcp', metric.value));
    75	        onINP((metric: any) => updateMetric('fid', metric.value));
    76	        onLCP((metric: any) => updateMetric('lcp', metric.value));
    77	        onTTFB((metric: any) => updateMetric('ttfb', metric.value));
    78	
    79	        setIsLoading(false);
    80	      })
    81	      .catch(() => {
    82	        setIsLoading(false);
    83	      });
    84	
    85	    return () => {
    86	      isMounted = false;
    87	      observersRef.current.forEach(observer => observer.disconnect());
    88	      observersRef.current = [];
    89	    };
    90	  }, [enabled]);
    91	
    92	  return { metrics, isLoading };
    93	};
    94	
    95	/**
    96	 * Dynamic Meta Tag Injection Hook
    97	 */
    98	const useDynamicMetaTags = (
    99	  metadata: SEOMetadata,
   100	  language: Language,
   101	  viewport: ViewportInfo | null
   102	) => {
   103	  const [dynamicTags, setDynamicTags] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});
   104	  const previousMetadataRef = useRef<SEOMetadata | null>(null);
   105	
   106	  useEffect(() => {
   107	    // Skip if metadata hasn't changed
   108	    if (previousMetadataRef.current === metadata) {
   109	      return;
   110	    }
   111	    previousMetadataRef.current = metadata;
   112	
   113	    // Generate dynamic tags based on context
   114	    const tags: Record<string, string> = {
   115	      'og:locale': language === 'zh-CN' ? 'zh_CN' : 'en_US',
   116	      'og:locale:alternate': language === 'zh-CN' ? 'en_US' : 'zh_CN',
   117	      'twitter:card': viewport?.isMobile ? 'summary' : 'summary_large_image',
   118	    };
   119	
   120	    // Add mobile-specific tags
   121	    if (viewport?.isMobile) {
   122	      tags['mobile-web-app-capable'] = 'yes';
   123	      tags['apple-mobile-web-app-capable'] = 'yes';
   124	      tags['apple-mobile-web-app-status-bar-style'] = 'default';
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    // Add performance hints
   128	    if ((viewport as any)?.connection) {
   129	      const { effectiveType } = (viewport as any).connection;
   130	      if (effectiveType === '2g' || effectiveType === 'slow-2g') {
   131	        tags['x-performance-mode'] = 'lite';
   132	      }
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    setDynamicTags(tags);
   136	  }, [metadata, language, viewport]);
   137	
   138	  return dynamicTags;
   139	};

   141	/**
   142	 * Enhanced SEO Manager Component
   143	 */
   144	export const EnhancedSEOManager: React.FC<SEOManagerProps> = ({
   145	  page = 'home',
   146	  language = 'zh-CN',
   147	  customMetadata,
   148	  enablePerformanceTracking = true,
   149	  enableStructuredData = true,
   150	  structuredDataTypes = ['WebApplication', 'BreadcrumbList'],
   151	  onMetadataGenerated,
   152	  onPerformanceUpdate,
   153	}) => {
   154	  // Use enhanced hooks (暂时注释避免未使用错误)
   155	  // const { isLoading } = useSEOConfig();
   156	  const viewport = useViewport();
   157	  const { metrics, isLoading: metricsLoading } =
   158	    useEnhancedSEOPerformance(enablePerformanceTracking);
   159	
   160	  // State for real-time updates
   161	  const [isHydrated, setIsHydrated] = useState(false);
   162	  const [structuredDataLoaded, setStructuredDataLoaded] = useState(false);
   163	
   164	  // Memoize metadata generation with dependency tracking
   165	  const metadata = useMemo(() => {
   166	    try {
   167	      const context = {
   168	        viewport,
   169	        performance: metrics,
   170	        language,
   171	        page,
   172	        isHydrated,
   173	      };
   174	
   175	      const generated = generatePageMetadata(page as PageType, context, language);
   176	      const merged = customMetadata ? { ...generated, ...customMetadata } : generated;
   177	
   178	      // Notify parent component
   179	      onMetadataGenerated?.(merged);
   180	
   181	      return merged;
   182	    } catch (error) {
   183	      console.error('[EnhancedSEOManager] Metadata generation failed:', error);
   184	      return generatePageMetadata('home', {}, language);
   185	    }
   186	  }, [page, language, customMetadata, viewport, metrics, isHydrated, onMetadataGenerated]);
   187	
   188	  // Convert ViewportState to ViewportInfo
   189	  const viewportInfo = viewport
   190	    ? {
   191	        ...viewport,
   192	        deviceType: viewport.isMobile
   193	          ? ('mobile' as const)
   194	          : viewport.isTablet
   195	            ? ('tablet' as const)
   196	            : ('desktop' as const),
   197	        orientation: viewport.isPortrait ? ('portrait' as const) : ('landscape' as const),
   198	      }
   199	    : null;
   200	
   201	  // Generate dynamic tags
   202	  const dynamicTags = useDynamicMetaTags(metadata, language, viewportInfo);
   203	
   204	  // Handle performance updates
   205	  useEffect(() => {
   206	    if (enablePerformanceTracking && !metricsLoading && onPerformanceUpdate) {
   207	      onPerformanceUpdate(metrics);
   208	    }
   209	  }, [metrics, metricsLoading, enablePerformanceTracking, onPerformanceUpdate]);
   210	
   211	  // Hydration detection
   212	  useEffect(() => {
   213	    setIsHydrated(true);
   214	  }, []);
   215	
   216	  // Generate canonical URL with locale
   217	  const canonicalUrl = useMemo(() => {
   218	    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return '';
   219	    const baseUrl = window.location.origin;
   220	    const path = window.location.pathname;
   221	    const locale = language === 'en' ? '/en' : '';
   222	    return `${baseUrl}${locale}${path}`;
   223	  }, [language]);
   224	
   225	  // Generate alternate language URLs
   226	  const alternateUrls = useMemo(() => {
   227	    if (typeof window === 'undefined') return [];
   228	    const baseUrl = window.location.origin;
   229	    const path = window.location.pathname;
   230	
   231	    return [
   232	      { lang: 'zh-CN', href: `${baseUrl}${path}` },
   233	      { lang: 'en', href: `${baseUrl}/en${path}` },
   234	    ];
   235	  }, []);
   236	
   237	  // Structured data generation with lazy loading
   238	  const structuredDataScripts = useMemo(() => {
   239	    if (!enableStructuredData || !structuredDataLoaded) return [];
   240	
   241	    return structuredDataTypes.map(type => ({
   242	      type: 'application/ld+json',
   243	      innerHTML: JSON.stringify({
   244	        '@context': 'https://schema.org',
   245	        '@type': type,
   246	        // This will be populated by the StructuredDataGenerator component
   247	        placeholder: true,
   248	      }),
   249	    }));
   250	  }, [enableStructuredData, structuredDataLoaded, structuredDataTypes]);
   251	
   252	  // Preconnect hints for performance
   253	  const preconnectHints = useMemo(
   254	    () => [
   255	      { rel: 'dns-prefetch', href: 'https://fonts.googleapis.com' },
   256	      { rel: 'dns-prefetch', href: 'https://www.googletagmanager.com' },
   257	      { rel: 'preconnect', href: 'https://fonts.gstatic.com', crossOrigin: 'anonymous' as const },
   258	    ],
   259	    []
   260	  );

   138	/**
   139	 * SEO Configuration Manager Class
   140	 * Provides robust configuration management with caching, validation, and hot-reload capabilities
   141	 */
   142	export class SEOConfigManager implements SEOConfigManagerInterface {
   143	  private config: SEOConfig | null = null;
   144	  private cache: SEOConfigCache = new Map();
   145	  private metrics: ConfigLoaderMetrics = {
   146	    loadCount: 0,
   147	    successCount: 0,
   148	    errorCount: 0,
   149	    avgLoadTime: 0,
   150	    lastLoadTime: 0,
   151	    totalLoadTime: 0,
   152	  };
   153	  private loadPromise: Promise<SEOConfigValidationResult> | null = null;
   154	  private readonly defaultConfigPath = '/src/config/seo.config.json';
   155	
   156	  /**
   157	   * Load and validate SEO configuration
   158	   */
   159	  async loadConfig(options: SEOConfigLoadOptions = {}): Promise<SEOConfigValidationResult> {
   160	    const startTime = performance.now();
   161	
   162	    try {
   163	      // Return existing promise if already loading
   164	      if (this.loadPromise && !options.force) {
   165	        return this.loadPromise;
   166	      }
   167	
   168	      // Return cached config if available and valid
   169	      if (this.config && !options.force && !options.validateOnly) {
   170	        return {
   171	          success: true,
   172	          config: this.config,
   173	          errors: [],
   174	          warnings: [],
   175	          loadTime: 0,
   176	        };
   177	      }
   178	
   179	      this.loadPromise = this._loadConfigInternal(options);
   180	      const result = await this.loadPromise;
   181	
   182	      const loadTime = performance.now() - startTime;
   183	      this._updateMetrics(result.success, loadTime);
   184	
   185	      return result;
   186	    } catch (error) {
   187	      const loadTime = performance.now() - startTime;
   188	      this._updateMetrics(false, loadTime);
   189	
   190	      return {
   191	        success: false,
   192	        errors: [
   193	          `Configuration load error: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error'}`,
   194	        ],
   195	        warnings: [],
   196	        loadTime,
   197	      };
   198	    } finally {
   199	      this.loadPromise = null;
   200	    }
   201	  }
   202	
   203	  /**
   204	   * Internal configuration loading logic
   205	   */
   206	  private async _loadConfigInternal(
   207	    options: SEOConfigLoadOptions
   208	  ): Promise<SEOConfigValidationResult> {
   209	    try {
   210	      // Dynamic import of configuration file
   211	      const configPath = options.configPath || this.defaultConfigPath;
   212	
   213	      let configData: unknown;
   214	
   215	      if (configPath.endsWith('.json')) {
   216	        // Load JSON configuration
   217	        const response = await fetch(configPath);
   218	        if (!response.ok) {
   219	          throw new Error(`Failed to load config from ${configPath}: ${response.statusText}`);
   220	        }
   221	        configData = await response.json();
   222	      } else {
   223	        // Dynamic import for TypeScript/JavaScript configs
   224	        const configModule = await import(configPath);
   225	        configData = configModule.default || configModule.SEO_CONFIG;
   226	      }
   227	
   228	      return this.validateConfig(configData);
   229	    } catch (error) {
   230	      return {
   231	        success: false,
   232	        errors: [
   233	          `Failed to load configuration: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error'}`,
   234	        ],
   235	        warnings: [],
   236	        loadTime: 0,
   237	      };
   238	    }
   239	  }
   240	
   241	  /**
   242	   * Comprehensive configuration validation
   243	   */
   244	  async validateConfig(configData: unknown): Promise<SEOConfigValidationResult> {
   245	    const errors: string[] = [];
   246	    const warnings: string[] = [];
   247	    const startTime = performance.now();
   248	
   249	    try {
   250	      if (!configData || typeof configData !== 'object') {
   251	        return {
   252	          success: false,
   253	          errors: ['Configuration data is null or not an object'],
   254	          warnings: [],
   255	          loadTime: performance.now() - startTime,
   256	        };
   257	      }
   258	
   259	      // Basic structure validation
   260	      this._validateBasicStructure(configData as Record<string, any>, errors);

===== src/config/seo.config.ts =====
     1	/**
     2	 * SEO配置桥接层 (Configuration Bridge)
     3	 *
     4	 * ⚠️ 重要说明:
     5	 * 这个文件现在是一个桥接层，实际配置请修改 src/config/seo.config.json
     6	 *
     7	 * 工作原理:
     8	 * 1. 优先从 seo.config.json 读取配置
     9	 * 2. 如果JSON配置不可用，回退到硬编码默认值
    10	 * 3. 保持与现有代码的向后兼容性
    11	 *
    12	 * 配置管理:
    13	 * - 主配置文件: src/config/seo.config.json
    14	 * - 类型定义: src/types/seo.types.ts
    15	 * - 配置管理器: src/utils/seo/SEOConfigManager.ts
    16	 */
    17	
    18	import { seoConfigManager } from '../utils/seo/SEOConfigManager';
    19	import type { SEOConfig } from '../types/seo.types';
    20	
    21	/**
    22	 * 动态获取配置 - 优先使用JSON配置，回退到硬编码配置
    23	 */
    24	function getConfigValue<T>(path: string, fallback: T): T {
    25	  try {
    26	    const config = seoConfigManager.getCurrentConfig();
    27	    if (!config) return fallback;
    28	
    29	    const keys = path.split('.');
    30	    let value = config as any;
    31	
    32	    for (const key of keys) {
    33	      if (value && typeof value === 'object' && key in value) {
    34	        value = value[key];
    35	      } else {
    36	        return fallback;
    37	      }
    38	    }
    39	
    40	    return value || fallback;
    41	  } catch {
    42	    return fallback;
    43	  }
    44	}
    45	
    46	// Legacy configuration object for backward compatibility

    48	export const SEO_CONFIG = {

    98	      longTail: ['如何分割长截图', '长截图怎么切割', '免费在线图片分割工具'],
    99	    };

   154	// 导出类型
   155	export type SEOConfigType = typeof SEO_CONFIG;
   156	export type SupportedLanguage = (typeof SEO_CONFIG.supportedLanguages)[number];
   157	export type PageKey = keyof typeof SEO_CONFIG.pages;

   160	/**
   161	 * Backward compatibility utilities
   162	 * These functions provide access to the new JSON-based configuration system
   163	 * while maintaining compatibility with existing code
   164	 */
   165	
   166	/**
   167	 * Initialize the new SEO configuration system
   168	 * Call this function during application startup
   169	 */
   170	export async function initializeSEOConfig(): Promise<void> {
   171	  try {
   172	    const result = await seoConfigManager.loadConfig({
   173	      validateOnly: false,
   174	      force: false,
   175	    });
   176	
   177	    if (!result.success) {
   178	      console.warn('SEO configuration failed to load:', result.errors);
   179	      console.info('Falling back to legacy configuration');
   180	    } else {
   181	      console.info('SEO configuration loaded successfully');
   182	    }
   183	  } catch (error) {
   184	    console.error('Failed to initialize SEO configuration:', error);
   185	    console.info('Using legacy configuration as fallback');
   186	  }
   187	}
   188	
   189	/**
   190	 * Get the current SEO configuration with fallback to legacy
   191	 */
   192	export function getCurrentSEOConfig(): SEOConfig | typeof SEO_CONFIG {
   193	  try {
   194	    const stats = seoConfigManager.getStats();
   195	    if (stats.loaded) {
   196	      return seoConfigManager.getConfig();
   197	    }
   198	  } catch {
   199	    console.warn('Failed to get current SEO config, using legacy fallback');
   200	  }
   201	
   202	  // Return legacy configuration as fallback
   203	  return SEO_CONFIG as any;
   204	}

===== src/types/index.ts =====
     1	// 应用状态类型定义
     2	
     3	export interface ImageSlice {
     4	  blob: Blob;
     5	  url: string;
     6	  index: number;
     7	  width: number;
     8	  height: number;
     9	}
    10	
    11	export interface AppState {
    12	  // Worker 相关状态
    13	  worker: Worker | null;
    14	  blobs: Blob[];
    15	  objectUrls: string[];
    16	
    17	  // 图片处理状态
    18	  originalImage: HTMLImageElement | null;
    19	  imageSlices: ImageSlice[];
    20	  selectedSlices: Set<number>;
    21	
    22	  // 处理状态
    23	  isProcessing: boolean;
    24	
    25	  // 元数据
    26	  splitHeight: number;
    27	  fileName: string;
    28	}
    29	
    30	export type AppAction =
    31	  | { type: 'SET_WORKER'; payload: Worker | null }
    32	  | { type: 'ADD_BLOB'; payload: { blob: Blob; index: number } }
    33	  | { type: 'SET_ORIGINAL_IMAGE'; payload: HTMLImageElement | null }
    34	  | { type: 'ADD_IMAGE_SLICE'; payload: ImageSlice }
    35	  | { type: 'TOGGLE_SLICE_SELECTION'; payload: number }
    36	  | { type: 'SELECT_ALL_SLICES' }
    37	  | { type: 'DESELECT_ALL_SLICES' }

     1	import { useState, useCallback } from 'react';
     2	import type { ImageProcessorHookReturn, AppState } from '../types';
     3	import { useWorker } from './useWorker';
     4	
     5	interface UseImageProcessorProps {
     6	  state: AppState;
     7	  actions: {
     8	    addBlob: (blob: Blob, index: number) => void;
     9	    addImageSlice: (slice: any) => void;
    10	    cleanupSession: () => void;
    11	    setProcessing: (isProcessing: boolean) => void;
    12	    setFileName: (name: string) => void;
    13	    setWorker: (worker: Worker | null) => void;
    14	    setOriginalImage: (image: HTMLImageElement | null) => void;
    15	    processingComplete: () => void;
    16	  };
    17	}
    18	
    19	export function useImageProcessor({
    20	  state,
    21	  actions,
    22	}: UseImageProcessorProps): ImageProcessorHookReturn {
    23	  const [progress, setProgress] = useState(0);
    24	
    25	  // Worker回调函数
    26	  const handleProgress = useCallback((workerProgress: number) => {
    27	    setProgress(workerProgress);
    28	  }, []);
    29	
    30	  const handleChunk = useCallback(
    31	    (blob: Blob, index: number) => {
    32	      console.log('[ImageProcessor] 收到图片切片:', index, blob.size);
    33	      // 添加Blob到状态
    34	      actions.addBlob(blob, index);
    35	
    36	      // 创建Object URL并添加图片切片
    37	      const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    38	      console.log('[ImageProcessor] 创建 Object URL:', url);
    39	
    40	      // 创建临时图片来获取尺寸
    41	      const img = new Image();
    42	      img.onload = () => {
    43	        console.log('[ImageProcessor] 图片加载完成，尺寸:', img.naturalWidth, img.naturalHeight);
    44	        console.log(
    45	          '[ImageProcessor] 添加图片切片到状态:',
    46	          index,
    47	          img.naturalWidth,
    48	          img.naturalHeight
    49	        );
    50	        const imageSlice = {
    51	          blob,
    52	          url,
    53	          index,
    54	          width: img.naturalWidth,
    55	          height: img.naturalHeight,
    56	        };
    57	        console.log('[ImageProcessor] 即将添加的图片切片对象:', imageSlice);
    58	        actions.addImageSlice(imageSlice);
    59	      };

    61	        console.error('[ImageProcessor] 图片加载失败:', error);
    62	      };
    63	      img.src = url;
    64	    },
    65	    [actions]
    66	  );
    67	
    68	  const handleDone = useCallback(() => {
    69	    console.log('[ImageProcessor] 图片处理完成');
    70	    actions.processingComplete();
    71	    setProgress(100);
    72	  }, [actions]);
    73	
    74	  const handleError = useCallback(
    75	    (message: string) => {
    76	      console.error('[ImageProcessor] Worker 错误:', message);
    77	      actions.setProcessing(false);
    78	      setProgress(0);
    79	    },
    80	    [actions]
    81	  );
    82	
    83	  // 使用Worker hook
    84	  const { createWorker, startProcessing } = useWorker({
    85	    onProgress: handleProgress,
    86	    onChunk: handleChunk,
    87	    onDone: handleDone,
    88	    onError: handleError,
    89	  });
    90	
    91	  // 处理图片
    92	  const processImage = useCallback(
    93	    async (file: File) => {
    94	      console.log('[ImageProcessor] 开始处理图片:', file.name);
    95	
    96	      // 清理之前的会话
    97	      actions.cleanupSession();
    98	      setProgress(0);
    99	
   100	      // 设置处理状态
   101	      actions.setProcessing(true);
   102	      actions.setFileName(file.name.replace(/\.[^/.]+$/, '') || '分割结果');

   104	      // 创建并设置原始图片
   105	      const img = new Image();
   106	      const imageUrl = URL.createObjectURL(file);
   107	
   108	      img.onload = () => {
   109	        console.log('[ImageProcessor] 原始图片加载完成，设置到状态中');
   110	        actions.setOriginalImage(img);
   111	        URL.revokeObjectURL(imageUrl); // 清理临时URL
   112	      };
   113	
   114	      img.onerror = error => {
   115	        console.error('[ImageProcessor] 原始图片加载失败:', error);
   116	        URL.revokeObjectURL(imageUrl);
   117	      };
   118	
   119	      img.src = imageUrl;

===== src/hooks/useWorker.ts (wc=     159) =====
     1	import { useCallback, useRef, useEffect } from 'react';
     2	import type { WorkerMessage } from '../types';
     3	
     4	export interface UseWorkerOptions {
     5	  onProgress?: (progress: number) => void;
     6	  onChunk?: (blob: Blob, index: number) => void;
     7	  onDone?: () => void;
     8	  onError?: (message: string) => void;
     9	}
    10	
    11	export interface UseWorkerReturn {
    12	  worker: Worker | null;
    13	  isWorkerReady: boolean;
    14	  startProcessing: (file: File, splitHeight: number) => void;
    15	  terminateWorker: () => void;
    16	  createWorker: () => void;
    17	}
    18	
    19	/**
    20	 * Web Worker管理Hook
    21	 * 提供Worker的创建、通信、生命周期管理功能
    22	 */
    23	export function useWorker(options: UseWorkerOptions = {}): UseWorkerReturn {
    24	  const workerRef = useRef<Worker | null>(null);
    25	  const isWorkerReadyRef = useRef(false);
    26	
    27	  const { onProgress, onChunk, onDone, onError } = options;
    28	
    29	  // 创建Worker
    30	  const createWorker = useCallback(() => {
    31	    try {
    32	      // 终止现有Worker
    33	      if (workerRef.current) {
    34	        workerRef.current.terminate();
    35	        workerRef.current = null;
    36	        isWorkerReadyRef.current = false;
    37	      }
    38	
    39	      // 创建新Worker
    40	      // type: 'module' 必需：worker 通过 ESM import splitAnalyzer，classic worker 不支持顶层 import。
    41	      // Vite 据此在 dev 用 module worker、build 打包为 ES module chunk。
    42	      workerRef.current = new Worker(new URL('../workers/split.worker.js', import.meta.url), {
    43	        type: 'module',
    44	      });
    45	
    46	      // 设置消息监听器
    47	      workerRef.current.onmessage = (event: MessageEvent<WorkerMessage>) => {
    48	        const { type, progress, blob, index, message } = event.data;
    49	
    50	        switch (type) {
    51	          case 'progress':
    52	            if (progress !== undefined && onProgress) {
    53	              onProgress(progress);
    54	            }
    55	            break;
    56	
    57	          case 'chunk':
    58	            if (blob && index !== undefined && onChunk) {
    59	              onChunk(blob, index);
    60	            }
    61	            break;
    62	
    63	          case 'done':
    64	            if (onDone) {
    65	              onDone();
    66	            }
    67	            break;
    68	
    69	          case 'error':
    70	            if (message && onError) {
    71	              onError(message);
    72	            }
    73	            break;
    74	
    75	          default:
    76	            console.warn('[useWorker] 未知的消息类型:', type);
    77	        }
    78	      };
    79	
    80	      // 设置错误监听器
    81	      workerRef.current.onerror = error => {
    82	        console.error('[useWorker] Worker错误:', error);
    83	        if (onError) {
    84	          onError(`Worker错误: ${error.message}`);
    85	        }
    86	      };
    87	
    88	      // 设置消息错误监听器
    89	      workerRef.current.onmessageerror = error => {
    90	        console.error('[useWorker] Worker消息错误:', error);
    91	        if (onError) {
    92	          onError('Worker消息传递错误');
    93	        }
    94	      };
    95	
    96	      isWorkerReadyRef.current = true;
    97	      console.log('[useWorker] Worker创建成功');
    98	    } catch (error) {
    99	      console.error('[useWorker] 创建Worker失败:', error);
   100	      if (onError) {
   101	        onError(`创建Worker失败: ${error instanceof Error ? error.message : '未知错误'}`);
   102	      }
   103	    }
   104	  }, [onProgress, onChunk, onDone, onError]);
   105	
   106	  // 终止Worker
   107	  const terminateWorker = useCallback(() => {
   108	    if (workerRef.current) {
   109	      try {
   110	        workerRef.current.terminate();
   111	        console.log('[useWorker] Worker已终止');
   112	      } catch (error) {
   113	        console.warn('[useWorker] 终止Worker时出错:', error);
   114	      } finally {
   115	        workerRef.current = null;
   116	        isWorkerReadyRef.current = false;
   117	      }
   118	    }
   119	  }, []);
   120	
===== src/workers/split.worker.js (wc=     264) =====
     1	// Message Contract (v1.1):
     2	// From Main to Worker: { file: File, splitHeight: number }
     3	// From Worker to Main:
     4	// - Progress: { type: 'progress', progress: number } // 0-100；分段：0-25 解码 / 25-30 内容感知分析 / 30-95 切片 / 100 完成
     5	// - Chunk:    { type: 'chunk', blob: Blob, index: number }
     6	// - Done:     { type: 'done' } // Simplified completion signal
     7	// - Error:    { type: 'error', message: string }
     8	//
     9	// 内容感知切割（spec §4）：解码后插入「分析」阶段，调用纯函数 splitAnalyzer
    10	// 得到切割点；有切割点则按点切，无则回退固定高度等分（绝不切得比现状差）。
    11	
    12	import { analyzeSplitPoints } from '../utils/splitAnalyzer';
    13	
    14	// Web Worker for handling image splitting operations
    15	// This worker runs in a separate thread to avoid blocking the UI
    16	
    17	/**
    18	 * 主消息监听器 - 接收来自主线程的消息
    19	 */
    20	self.onmessage = function (event) {
    21	  try {
    22	    const { file, splitHeight } = event.data;
    23	
    24	    // 参数验证
    25	    if (!file) {
    26	      self.postMessage({
    27	        type: 'error',
    28	        message: 'No file provided',
    29	      });
    30	      return;
    31	    }
    32	
    33	    if (!(file instanceof File)) {
    34	      self.postMessage({
    35	        type: 'error',
    36	        message: 'Invalid file object provided',
    37	      });
    38	      return;
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    if (!splitHeight || typeof splitHeight !== 'number' || splitHeight <= 0) {
    42	      self.postMessage({
    43	        type: 'error',
    44	        message: 'Invalid splitHeight provided. Must be a positive number.',
    45	      });
    46	      return;
    47	    }
    48	
    49	    // 验证文件类型
    50	    if (!file.type.startsWith('image/')) {
    51	      self.postMessage({
    52	        type: 'error',
    53	        message: 'File must be an image',
    54	      });
    55	      return;
    56	    }
    57	
    58	    console.log(`Worker received: ${file.name}, splitHeight: ${splitHeight}`);
    59	
    60	    // 开始图片处理流程
    61	    processImage(file, splitHeight);
    62	  } catch (error) {
    63	    console.error('Worker error:', error);
    64	    self.postMessage({
    65	      type: 'error',
    66	      message: `Worker processing error: ${error.message}`,
    67	    });
    68	  }
    69	};
    70	
    71	/**
    72	 * 图片处理主函数
    73	 * 流程：解码 → 全图绘制 → 内容感知分析（得切割点）→ 按切割点切片（无切割点则等分回退）
    74	 */
    75	async function processImage(file, splitHeight) {
    76	  try {
    77	    // 发送初始进度
    78	    self.postMessage({
    79	      type: 'progress',
    80	      progress: 0,
    81	    });
    82	
    83	    console.log('Starting image processing...');
    84	
    85	    // 使用 createImageBitmap 解码图片
    86	    console.log('Decoding image with createImageBitmap...');
    87	    const imageBitmap = await createImageBitmap(file);
    88	
    89	    console.log(
    90	      `Image decoded successfully. Dimensions: ${imageBitmap.width} x ${imageBitmap.height}`
    91	    );
    92	
    93	    // 创建 OffscreenCanvas 并设置其尺寸与原图一致
    94	    const canvas = new OffscreenCanvas(imageBitmap.width, imageBitmap.height);
    95	    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
    96	
    97	    console.log(`OffscreenCanvas created with dimensions: ${canvas.width} x ${canvas.height}`);
    98	
    99	    // 将图片位图绘制到 OffscreenCanvas 上
   100	    ctx.drawImage(imageBitmap, 0, 0);
   101	
   102	    // 更新进度到 25% (图片解码和绘制完成)
   103	    self.postMessage({
   104	      type: 'progress',
   105	      progress: 25,
   106	    });
   107	
   108	    // 释放 imageBitmap 资源
   109	    imageBitmap.close();
   110	
   111	    // 内容感知分析：读取全图像素，计算切割点
   112	    // 注：当前为全图 getImageData（KISS）；大图（>4000px）分块读取为未来优化项（spec §4.6）
   113	    console.log('Analyzing content for split points...');
   114	    let splitPoints = [];
   115	    try {
   116	      const imageData = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
   117	      splitPoints = analyzeSplitPoints(imageData.data, canvas.width, canvas.height, {
   118	        targetHeight: splitHeight,
   119	      });
   120	      console.log(
===== src/utils/splitAnalyzer.ts (wc=     279) =====
     1	/**
     2	 * 内容感知切割分析器（Content-Aware Split Analyzer）
     3	 *
     4	 * 设计依据：docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-25-content-aware-split-design.md §4
     5	 *
     6	 * 核心原则：算法与 I/O 分离。本模块全部为纯函数，无 DOM/canvas/Worker 依赖，
     7	 * 可独立单测。Worker 仅负责 decode/getImageData/drawImage 胶水并调用本模块。
     8	 *
     9	 * 流水线（spec §4.2 不变量）：
    10	 *   压成行信号 → 去噪 → 找空白带 → 页高驱动选点 → 最小间距保护 → 无解安全回退
    11	 *
    12	 * ⚠️ thresholdRatio / minBandHeight / smoothingWindow 为起始经验值（spec §4.4），
    13	 *    必须用真实长截图校准后回填，不可拍脑袋定死。
    14	 */
    15	
    16	/** 低变化水平带：一段连续的「内容空白」行区间 */
    17	export interface Band {
    18	  /** 起始行（inclusive） */
    19	  top: number;
    20	  /** 结束行（exclusive） */
    21	  bottom: number;
    22	  /** 带中心行，作为切割点候选 */
    23	  center: number;
    24	}
    25	
    26	/**
    27	 * 分析阶段全部可调参数（ratio 形式以适配不同尺寸图片）。
    28	 * 默认值见 DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS。
    29	 */
    30	export interface SplitOptions {
    31	  /** 目标页高（复用现有 splitHeight 语义） */
    32	  targetHeight: number;
    33	  /** 列降采样步长，越大越快、精度越低 */
    34	  columnStep: number;
    35	  /** 低变化阈值倍数：阈值 = mean(profile) × thresholdRatio */
    36	  thresholdRatio: number;
    37	  /** 平滑窗口大小（行），约一行行距；1 表示不平滑 */
    38	  smoothingWindow: number;
    39	  /** 空白带最小高度（行），用于过滤噪声细缝 */
    40	  minBandHeight: number;
    41	  /** 搜索范围占 targetHeight 的比例（±） */
    42	  searchWindowRatio: number;
    43	  /** 最小切割间距占 targetHeight 的比例，防碎页 */
    44	  mergeRatio: number;
    45	  /** 单页最小高度占 targetHeight 的比例，末页合并依据 */
    46	  minPageRatio: number;
    47	}
    48	
    49	/** 默认参数（spec §4.3，部分为起始经验值，待校准） */
    50	export const DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS: SplitOptions = {
    51	  targetHeight: 1200,
    52	  columnStep: 4,
    53	  thresholdRatio: 0.3,
    54	  smoothingWindow: 8,
    55	  minBandHeight: 8,
    56	  searchWindowRatio: 0.2,
    57	  mergeRatio: 0.5,
    58	  minPageRatio: 0.5,
    59	};
    60	
    61	/** chooseSplitPoints 的参数（已由 ratio 换算为像素绝对值） */
    62	export interface ChoosePointsOptions {
    63	  /** 目标页高 */
    64	  targetHeight: number;
    65	  /** 搜索范围（±像素） */
    66	  searchWindow: number;
    67	  /** 最小切割间距（像素） */
    68	  mergeThreshold: number;
    69	  /** 单页最小高度（像素） */
    70	  minPageHeight: number;
    71	  /** 图像总高度 */
    72	  imageHeight: number;
    73	}
    74	
    75	/**
    76	 * 计算行级水平变化率（spec §4.2 第 1 步）。
    77	 *
    78	 * 对每行 y：在采样列上累加水平相邻像素的【灰度差绝对值】。
    79	 * 灰度 = 0.299R + 0.587G + 0.114B；行变化率反映该行内容密度，
    80	 * 文字行高、空白行接近 0。变化率不依赖背景色检测，对多背景图更鲁棒。
    81	 *
    82	 * @param pixels   RGBA 像素数据（每像素 4 字节）
    83	 * @param width    图像宽度（像素）
    84	 * @param height   图像高度（像素）
    85	 * @param columnStep 列降采样步长（默认 4，计算量降至 1/columnStep）
    86	 * @returns 长度为 height 的数组，profile[y] = 第 y 行的总变化率
    87	 */
    88	export function computeVariationProfile(
    89	  pixels: Uint8ClampedArray | Uint8Array,
    90	  width: number,
    91	  height: number,
    92	  columnStep: number = DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS.columnStep
    93	): number[] {
    94	  const profile: number[] = new Array(height).fill(0);
    95	  const step = Math.max(1, Math.floor(columnStep));
    96	
    97	  for (let y = 0; y < height; y++) {
    98	    const rowBase = y * width;
    99	    let variation = 0;
   100	    // 采样列 x = step, 2·step, ...，比较像素 x 与其左邻 x-1 的灰度差
   101	    for (let x = step; x < width; x += step) {
   102	      const idxCurr = (rowBase + x) * 4;
   103	      const idxPrev = (rowBase + x - 1) * 4;
   104	      const grayCurr =
   105	        0.299 * pixels[idxCurr] + 0.587 * pixels[idxCurr + 1] + 0.114 * pixels[idxCurr + 2];
   106	      const grayPrev =
   107	        0.299 * pixels[idxPrev] + 0.587 * pixels[idxPrev + 1] + 0.114 * pixels[idxPrev + 2];
   108	      variation += Math.abs(grayCurr - grayPrev);
   109	    }
   110	    profile[y] = variation;
   111	  }
   112	  return profile;
   113	}
   114	
   115	/**
   116	 * 居中滑动平均平滑（spec §4.2 第 2 步）。
   117	 * 消除单行噪声；windowSize=1 时原样返回（不平滑）。边界处只取存在的邻居。
   118	 *
   119	 * @param profile    变化率曲线
   120	 * @param windowSize 窗口大小（行）；越大越平滑

    10	  /** 页面格式 */

    20	}

    22	/**
    23	 * 默认PDF导出配置
    24	 */
    25	const DEFAULT_OPTIONS: Required<PDFExportOptions> = {
    26	  orientation: 'portrait',
    27	  format: 'a4',
    28	  quality: 0.8,
    29	  margin: 10,
    30	  autoResize: true,
    31	  imagesPerPage: 1,
    32	};

    34	/**
    35	 * PDF导出器类
    36	 */
    37	export class PDFExporter {
    38	  private options: Required<PDFExportOptions>;
    39	
    40	  constructor(options: PDFExportOptions = {}) {
    41	    this.options = { ...DEFAULT_OPTIONS, ...options };
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  /**
    45	   * 导出图片切片为PDF
    46	   * @param imageSlices 图片切片数组
    47	   * @param selectedIndices 选中的切片索引
    48	   * @param fileName 文件名
    49	   * @param onProgress 进度回调
    50	   */
    51	  async exportToPDF(
    52	    imageSlices: ImageSlice[],
    53	    selectedIndices: Set<number>,
    54	    fileName: string = 'exported-images',
    55	    onProgress?: (progress: number) => void
    56	  ): Promise<void> {
    57	    try {
    58	      // 过滤选中的切片
    59	      const selectedSlices = imageSlices
    60	        .filter(slice => selectedIndices.has(slice.index))
    61	        .sort((a, b) => a.index - b.index);
    62	
    63	      if (selectedSlices.length === 0) {
    64	        throw new Error('没有选中的图片切片');
    65	      }
    66	
    67	      // 创建PDF文档
    68	      const pdf = new jsPDF({
    69	        orientation: this.options.orientation,
    70	        unit: 'mm',
    71	        format: this.options.format,
    72	      });
    73	
    74	      // 获取页面尺寸
    75	      const pageWidth = pdf.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
    76	      const pageHeight = pdf.internal.pageSize.getHeight();
    77	      const contentWidth = pageWidth - this.options.margin * 2;
    78	      const contentHeight = pageHeight - this.options.margin * 2;
    79	
    80	      let imagesOnCurrentPage = 0;
    81	
    82	      for (let i = 0; i < selectedSlices.length; i++) {
    83	        const slice = selectedSlices[i];
    84	
    85	        // 如果需要新页面
    86	        if (imagesOnCurrentPage >= this.options.imagesPerPage) {
    87	          pdf.addPage();
    88	          imagesOnCurrentPage = 0;
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        // 如果是第一张图片，不需要添加页面
    92	        if (i === 0) {
    93	          // 第一页已经存在
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        try {
    97	          // 将Blob转换为base64
    98	          const imageData = await this.blobToBase64(slice.blob);
    99	
   100	          // 计算图片尺寸
   101	          const { width, height } = this.calculateImageSize(
   102	            slice.width,
   103	            slice.height,
   104	            contentWidth,
   105	            contentHeight
   106	          );
   107	
   108	          // 计算图片位置（居中）
   109	          const x = this.options.margin + (contentWidth - width) / 2;
   110	          const y =
   111	            this.options.margin +
   112	            imagesOnCurrentPage * (contentHeight / this.options.imagesPerPage);
   113	
   114	          // 添加图片到PDF
   115	          pdf.addImage(imageData, 'JPEG', x, y, width, height, undefined, 'FAST');
   116	
   117	          imagesOnCurrentPage++;
   118	
   119	          // 更新进度
   120	          if (onProgress) {

    20	/**
    21	 * 默认ZIP导出配置

    23	const DEFAULT_OPTIONS: Required<ZIPExportOptions> = {
    24	  compressionLevel: 6,
    25	  fileNameFormat: 'sequence',
    26	  fileNamePrefix: 'slice',
    27	  imageFormat: 'original',
    28	  jpegQuality: 0.8,
    29	};
    30	
    31	/**
    32	 * ZIP导出器类
    33	 */
    34	export class ZIPExporter {
    35	  private options: Required<ZIPExportOptions>;
    36	
    37	  constructor(options: ZIPExportOptions = {}) {
    38	    this.options = { ...DEFAULT_OPTIONS, ...options };
    39	  }
    40	
    41	  /**
    42	   * 导出图片切片为ZIP
    43	   */
    44	  async exportToZIP(
    45	    imageSlices: ImageSlice[],
    46	    selectedIndices: Set<number>,
    47	    fileName: string = 'exported-images',
    48	    onProgress?: (progress: number) => void
    49	  ): Promise<void> {
    50	    try {
    51	      const selectedSlices = imageSlices
    52	        .filter(slice => selectedIndices.has(slice.index))
    53	        .sort((a, b) => a.index - b.index);
    54	
    55	      if (selectedSlices.length === 0) {
    56	        throw new Error('没有选中的图片切片');
    57	      }
    58	
    59	      const zip = new JSZip();
    60	
    61	      for (let i = 0; i < selectedSlices.length; i++) {
    62	        const slice = selectedSlices[i];
    63	
    64	        try {
    65	          const imageFileName = this.generateFileName(slice, i);
    66	          const processedBlob = await this.processImageFormat(slice.blob);
    67	          zip.file(imageFileName, processedBlob);
    68	
    69	          if (onProgress) {
    70	            const progress = Math.round(((i + 1) / selectedSlices.length) * 80);
    71	            onProgress(progress);
    72	          }
    73	        } catch (error) {
    74	          console.warn(`处理图片切片 ${slice.index} 时出错:`, error);
    75	          continue;
    76	        }
    77	      }
    78	
    79	      if (onProgress) {
    80	        onProgress(85);
    81	      }
    82	
    83	      const zipBlob = await zip.generateAsync({
    84	        type: 'blob',
    85	        compression: 'DEFLATE',
    86	        compressionOptions: {
    87	          level: this.options.compressionLevel,
    88	        },
    89	      });
    90	
    91	      if (onProgress) {
    92	        onProgress(95);
    93	      }
    94	
    95	      const zipFileName = fileName.endsWith('.zip') ? fileName : `${fileName}.zip`;
    96	      this.downloadBlob(zipBlob, zipFileName);
    97	
    98	      if (onProgress) {
    99	        onProgress(100);
   100	      }
   101	
   102	      console.log(`ZIP导出完成: ${zipFileName}`);
   103	    } catch (error) {
   104	      console.error('ZIP导出失败:', error);
   105	      throw error;
   106	    }
   107	  }
   108	
   109	  private generateFileName(slice: ImageSlice, sequenceIndex: number): string {
   110	    const extension = this.getFileExtension(slice.blob.type);
   111	
   112	    switch (this.options.fileNameFormat) {
   113	      case 'index':
   114	        return `${this.options.fileNamePrefix}_${slice.index}.${extension}`;
   115	      case 'sequence':
   116	        return `${this.options.fileNamePrefix}_${String(sequenceIndex + 1).padStart(3, '0')}.${extension}`;
   117	      case 'custom':
   118	        return `${this.options.fileNamePrefix}_${slice.index}_${sequenceIndex + 1}.${extension}`;
   119	      default:
   120	        return `${this.options.fileNamePrefix}_${sequenceIndex + 1}.${extension}`;

    85	    const imageSlicesLength = appState.imageSlices.length;
    86	    const selectedSlicesSize = appState.selectedSlices.size;
    87	    const isProcessing = appState.isProcessing || false;
    88

    90	      hasOriginalImage,
    91	      hasImageSlices: imageSlicesLength > 0,
    92	      hasSelectedSlices: selectedSlicesSize > 0,
    93	      imageSlicesLength,
    94	      selectedSlicesSize,
    95	      isProcessing,
    96	    };
    97	  }, [
    98	    appState.originalImage,
    99	    appState.imageSlices.length,
   100	    appState.selectedSlices.size,
   101	    appState.isProcessing,
   102	  ]);
   103	
   104	  // 计算导航项状态，使用useMemo优化
   105	  const navigationItems = useMemo(() => {
   106	    const { hasOriginalImage, hasSelectedSlices, isProcessing } = keyStates;
   107	
   108	    return DEFAULT_NAVIGATION_ITEMS.map(item => {
   109	      let disabled = false;
   110	      const active = currentPath === item.path;
   111	
   112	      // 根据路径和应用状态确定是否禁用
   113	      switch (item.path) {
   114	        case '/':
   115	        case '/upload':
   116	          disabled = isProcessing;
   117	          break;
   118	        case '/split':
   119	          disabled = !hasOriginalImage || isProcessing;
   120	          break;

    16	/**
    17	 * 性能优化钩子
    18	 * 监控页面性能并优化SEO元数据加载
    19	 */
    20	const useSEOPerformance = () => {
    21	  const [metrics, setMetrics] = useState<PerformanceMetrics | null>(null);
    22	  const observerRef = useRef<PerformanceObserver | null>(null);
    23	
    24	  useEffect(() => {
    25	    // 创建性能观察器
    26	    if (typeof window !== 'undefined' && 'PerformanceObserver' in window) {
    27	      try {
    28	        observerRef.current = new PerformanceObserver(list => {
    29	          const entries = list.getEntries();
    30	          let fcp = 0,
    31	            lcp = 0,
    32	            fid = 0,
    33	            cls = 0,
    34	            ttfb = 0;
    35	
    36	          entries.forEach(entry => {
    37	            if (entry.name === 'first-contentful-paint') {
    38	              fcp = entry.startTime;
    39	            } else if (entry.entryType === 'largest-contentful-paint') {
    40	              lcp = entry.startTime;
    41	            } else if (entry.entryType === 'first-input') {
    42	              fid = (entry as any).processingStart - entry.startTime;
    43	            } else if (entry.entryType === 'layout-shift') {
    44	              cls += (entry as any).value;
    45	            } else if (entry.entryType === 'navigation') {
    46	              ttfb = (entry as any).responseStart;
    47	            }
    48	          });
    49	
    50	          setMetrics({ fcp, lcp, fid, cls, ttfb });
    51	        });
    52	
    53	        // 观察多种性能指标
    54	        observerRef.current.observe({
    55	          entryTypes: [
    56	            'paint',
    57	            'largest-contentful-paint',
    58	            'first-input',
    59	            'layout-shift',
    60	            'navigation',
    61	          ],
    62	        });
    63	      } catch (error) {
    64	        console.warn('Performance observation not supported:', error);
    65	      }
    66	    }
    67	
    68	    return () => {
    69	      if (observerRef.current) {
    70	        observerRef.current.disconnect();
    71	      }
    72	    };
    73	  }, []);
    74	
    75	  return metrics;
    76	};

    82	const useViewportDetection = (): ViewportInfo => {
    83	  const [viewportInfo, setViewportInfo] = useState<ViewportInfo>({
    84	    width: 0,
    85	    height: 0,
    86	    deviceType: 'desktop',
    87	    isMobile: false,
    88	    isTablet: false,
    89	    isDesktop: true,
    90	    orientation: 'landscape',
    91	  });
    92	
    93	  useEffect(() => {
    94	    const updateViewport = () => {
    95	      const width = window.innerWidth;
    96	      const height = window.innerHeight;
    97	      const isMobile = width < 768;
    98	      const isTablet = width >= 768 && width < 1024;
    99	      const isDesktop = width >= 1024;
   100	
   101	      setViewportInfo({
   102	        width,
   103	        height,
   104	        deviceType: isMobile ? 'mobile' : isTablet ? 'tablet' : 'desktop',
   105	        isMobile,
   106	        isTablet,
   107	        isDesktop,
   108	        orientation: width > height ? 'landscape' : 'portrait',
   109	      });
   110	    };
   111	
   112	    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
   113	      updateViewport();
   114	      window.addEventListener('resize', updateViewport);
   115	      window.addEventListener('orientationchange', updateViewport);
   116	
   117	      return () => {
   118	        window.removeEventListener('resize', updateViewport);
   119	        window.removeEventListener('orientationchange', updateViewport);
   120	      };

   218	/**
   219	 * 根据切割点计算切片边界 [[startY, endY], ...]（spec §4.5）
   220	 * - 有切割点：按切割点分段，保证每段落在内容空白带之间
   221	 * - 无切割点：回退固定高度等分（与原逻辑一致，绝不切得比现状差）
   222	 *
   223	 * @param {number[]} splitPoints 切割点 y 坐标数组（来自 splitAnalyzer）
   224	 * @param {number} imageHeight   图像总高度
   225	 * @param {number} splitHeight   等分回退时的固定页高
   226	 * @returns {Array<[number, number]>} 切片边界数组
   227	 */
   228	function computeSliceBounds(splitPoints, imageHeight, splitHeight) {
   229	  // 内容感知：按切割点分段
   230	  if (splitPoints.length > 0) {
   231	    const bounds = [];
   232	    let prev = 0;
   233	    for (const point of splitPoints) {
   234	      bounds.push([prev, point]);
   235	      prev = point;
   236	    }
   237	    bounds.push([prev, imageHeight]);
   238	    return bounds;
   239	  }
   240	
   241	  // 等分回退：固定高度等分（与原 split.worker.js 行为完全一致）
   242	  const bounds = [];
   243	  const totalChunks = Math.ceil(imageHeight / splitHeight);
   244	  for (let i = 0; i < totalChunks; i++) {
   245	    const startY = i * splitHeight;
   246	    const endY = Math.min(startY + splitHeight, imageHeight);
   247	    bounds.push([startY, endY]);
   248	  }
   249	  return bounds;
   250	}

   253	 * 将 OffscreenCanvas 转换为 Blob

   255	 * @param {string} type - 图片类型 (如 'image/jpeg')
   256	 * @param {number} quality - 图片质量 (0-1)，默认 0.92（减轻文字振铃伪影）
   257	 * @returns {Promise<Blob>} - 转换后的 Blob 对象
   258	 */
   259	async function convertToBlob(canvas, type = 'image/jpeg', quality = 0.92) {
   260	  return await canvas.convertToBlob({
   261	    type: type,
   262	    quality: quality,
   263	  });
   264	}

   231	    points.pop();
   232	  }
   233	
   234	  return points;
   235	}
   236	
   237	/**
   238	 * 内容感知切割分析入口（封装 spec §4.2 全流程）。
   239	 *
   240	 * Worker 调用此函数：传入全图像素 + 尺寸，返回切割点数组。
   241	 * 返回空数组表示「不切」（图片过短）或「无合格空白带需等分回退」——
   242	 * 调用方对空数组应回退到固定高度等分（spec §4.5）。
   243	 *
   244	 * @param pixels  RGBA 像素数据
   245	 * @param width   图像宽度
   246	 * @param height  图像高度
   247	 * @param options 可选参数覆盖（缺省用 DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS）
   248	 * @returns 切割点 y 坐标数组；空表示需等分回退或不切
   249	 */
   250	export function analyzeSplitPoints(
   251	  pixels: Uint8ClampedArray | Uint8Array,
   252	  width: number,
   253	  height: number,
   254	  options?: Partial<SplitOptions>
   255	): number[] {
   256	  const opts = { ...DEFAULT_SPLIT_OPTIONS, ...options };
   257	
   258	  // 图片短于目标页高 → 不切
   259	  if (height <= opts.targetHeight) {
   260	    return [];
   261	  }
   262	
   263	  // 1. 行变化率
   264	  const profile = computeVariationProfile(pixels, width, height, opts.columnStep);
   265	  // 2. 平滑去噪
   266	  const smoothed = smooth(profile, opts.smoothingWindow);
   267	  // 3. 相对阈值：低于变化率均值的 thresholdRatio 倍视为「低变化」
   268	  const mean = profile.reduce((acc, v) => acc + v, 0) / Math.max(1, profile.length);
   269	  const threshold = mean * opts.thresholdRatio;
   270	  const bands = findLowVariationBands(smoothed, threshold, opts.minBandHeight);
   271	  // 4. 页高驱动选点
   272	  return chooseSplitPoints(bands, {
   273	    targetHeight: opts.targetHeight,
   274	    searchWindow: Math.round(opts.targetHeight * opts.searchWindowRatio),
   275	    mergeThreshold: Math.round(opts.targetHeight * opts.mergeRatio),
   276	    minPageHeight: Math.round(opts.targetHeight * opts.minPageRatio),
   277	    imageHeight: height,
   278	  });
   279	}
   180	    return { width, height };
   181	  }
   182	
   183	  /**
   184	   * 更新导出选项
   185	   */
   186	  updateOptions(options: Partial<PDFExportOptions>): void {
   187	    this.options = { ...this.options, ...options };
   188	  }
   189	
   190	  /**
   191	   * 获取当前配置
   192	   */
   193	  getOptions(): Required<PDFExportOptions> {
   194	    return { ...this.options };
   195	  }
   196	}
   197	
   198	/**
   199	 * 创建默认PDF导出器实例
   200	 */
   201	export const createPDFExporter = (options?: PDFExportOptions) => {

# 系统架构文档

## 📋 架构概述

长截图分割器采用现代化的**扁平化单仓库架构**，基于 React 18 + TypeScript + Vite 技术栈构建，注重性能、可维护性和用户体验。

---

## 🏗️ 架构决策记录 (ADR)

### ADR-001: 架构模式选择

**状态**: 已采纳  
**日期**: 2025-08-25  
**决策者**: 开发团队

**背景**: 项目初期考虑了多种架构模式，包括多仓库微前端、单仓库模块化等方案。

**决策**: 采用扁平化单仓库架构

**理由**:

1. **项目规模适中**: 功能相对集中，不需要复杂的微服务架构
2. **开发效率优先**: 减少跨仓库协调成本，统一开发环境
3. **维护成本考虑**: 单一构建配置，降低运维复杂度
4. **团队协作**: 简化版本管理和发布流程

**后果**:

- ✅ 开发效率提升，构建速度快
- ✅ 依赖管理简化，版本冲突减少
- ✅ 代码审查和质量控制更容易
- ⚠️ 需要良好的模块边界设计
- ⚠️ 大型团队可能面临代码冲突

---

def role_for(file: str, symbol: str, typ: str) -> str:
    if file in PRIORITY:
        base = PRIORITY[file]
        return f\"{base} 符号 {symbol}（{typ}）参与该文件职责。\"
    if file.startswith(\"src/utils/seo/\") or \"/seo/\" in file or \"SEO\" in file or \"seo.\" in file:
        return f\"SEO 子系统单元 {symbol}：配置/元数据/结构化数据相关实现，服务于页面可发现性而非切图主链。\"
    if \"navigat\" in file.lower() or \"Navigation\" in symbol or \"Router\" in symbol:
        return f\"导航相关单元 {symbol}：步骤可用性/路径守卫/错误恢复，约束用户在 upload→split→export 间的可达性。\"
    if \"export\" in file.lower() or \"Export\" in symbol or \"pdf\" in file.lower() or \"zip\" in file.lower():
        return f\"导出边界单元 {symbol}：把选中切片转为 PDF/ZIP 下载，旁路于 Worker 切图状态机。\"
    if \"worker\" in file.lower() or \"Worker\" in symbol or \"split\" in file.lower():
        return f\"切图/Worker 相关单元 {symbol}：参与离主线程计算或切片数据结构。\"
    if file.startswith(\"src/hooks/\"):
        return f\"业务 Hook {symbol}：封装 React 状态/副作用，向 UI 暴露能力而不直接做像素切割。\"
    if file.startswith(\"src/components/\"):
        return f\"UI 组件单元 {symbol}：呈现上传/预览/导出/导航交互，状态仍由 hooks 拥有。\"
    if file.startswith(\"src/utils/\"):
        return f\"工具单元 {symbol}：为运行时提供纯函数或副作用服务（性能/缓存/错误/格式）。\"
    if file.startswith(\"src/types/\"):
        return f\"类型契约 {symbol}：稳定跨模块接口，约束状态与消息形状。\"
    if file.startswith(\"src/config/\") or file.startswith(\"config/\"):
        return f\"配置单元 {symbol}：聚合应用/环境/常量参数，不拥有会话状态。\"
    if file.startswith(\"shared-components/\"):
        return f\"共享组件单元 {symbol}：可复用 UI/通信管理，被主应用引用。\"
    if file.startswith(\"tools/\"):
        return f\"构建工具单元 {symbol}：工程侧构建/部署/优化脚本。\"
    if file.startswith(\"scripts/\"):
        return f\"脚本单元 {symbol}：开发/SEO 生成工作流，非产品主数据流。\"
    if file.startswith(\"src/\"):
        return f\"src 运行时单元 {symbol}：参与产品功能或支撑能力。\"
    return f\"模块单元 {symbol}：次要/支撑职责。\"
